**Last updated:** Sprint 11.5 (2026-05-18) — MCQ + Mini Test + content browser + analytics (DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE foundation 5/5 — **CLUSTER CLOSED**). Ships the final 2 exercise modes + the surfaces that make the module usable as a complete IELTS Listening skill. **Backend:** migration 059 (`listening_sessions` gains `session_type` discriminator + `exercise_ids UUID[]` lineup + `ordered_position JSONB` scaffold metadata; legacy `section_content_ids` retained for backward compat); `routers/listening.py` extends to dispatch `mode='mcq'` (new `_grade_and_save_mcq` strips canonical `answer_idx` from client response, persists full details server-side); new browse endpoint `GET /api/listening/content` (accent_tag + cefr_level + ielts_section filters, published only, no signed URL in payload); analytics endpoint `GET /api/listening/analytics?range=7d|30d|all` (per-mode count/avg_score/accuracy, 14-day bar chart, recent 10 attempts, weakest-mode requires ≥3 attempts per CLAUDE.md non-misleading rule). **Frontend:** 6 new pages + JS — `listening-mcq.html`/.js (user, A/B/C/D radio, strips answer_idx client-side), `admin-listening-mcq.html`/.js (1-20 question authoring with per-question correct-answer radio), `listening-mini-test.html`/.js (runner walking exercise_ids[] sequentially, per-step dispatch by exercise_type, summary with correct/total/score/band), `admin-listening-mini-test.html`/.js (click-to-add pool → reorderable lineup → POST sessions), `listening-browse.html`/.js (4-mode deep links per content card), `listening-analytics.html`/.js (range tabs + summary cards + per-mode table + 14-day chart + recent activity + Vietnamese mode labels). Landing page: MCQ + Mini Test cards promoted to LIVE (5/5 active), browse + analytics utility links added. **+31 backend tests** (5 MCQ grader unit + 6 MCQ payload validator + 3 MCQ dispatch + 4 admin session create + 2 user session get + 3 session complete/band + 3 browse + 5 analytics). **+39 frontend sentinels** (6-page contract + cross-cutting design-token discipline + updated listening-page-shell pins for 5-LIVE roster + browse/analytics utility links). **Backend pytest: 1147 passed** (+31 vs 11.4 baseline 1116). **Frontend node tests: 2806 passed** (+37 vs 11.4 baseline 2769, after listening-page-shell roster pin update). **No new audit hotfixes — count unchanged at 25.** **DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE foundation phase COMPLETE** — 5 modes shipped end-to-end (dictation 11.2 → segmented v2 11.3 + 11.3.1-hotfix → gist + T/F 11.4 + ElevenLabs alignment → MCQ + Mini Test + browse + analytics 11.5). **Last updated:** Sprint 11.4 (2026-05-18) — Gist + True/False exercises + ElevenLabs word-level alignment (DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE foundation 4/5). Ships 2 new exercise modes (Gist via Haiku semantic grading, T/F/NG with IELTS 3-state convention) end-to-end: backend graders + payload validators + router mode-dispatch, 4 new pages (admin authoring + user surface for each), landing card promotion (3 cards live now: dictation/gist/tf; 2 deferred: mcq/mini-test). **P1 BONUS shipped:** renderer switched to ElevenLabs `/v1/text-to-speech/{voice_id}/with-timestamps` endpoint; alignment_data persisted to new `listening_content.alignment_data JSONB` (migration 058); admin segment editor prefers alignment-driven timestamps (sub-50ms boundaries, ✨ AI-precision banner) and falls back to 11.3.1 char-proportional when alignment absent (📐 estimate banner) — fully backward-compatible for legacy MP3 uploads + pre-11.4 renders. Backend: `services/listening_gist_grader.py` (Haiku 4.5 with `_call_with_retry` + fail-soft keyword-coverage fallback); `services/listening_grader.grade_true_false()` helper with T/F/NG/TRUE/FALSE normalisation; admin upsert payload validators `_validate_gist_payload` + `_validate_true_false_payload` (3-12 statement range, contiguous idx, answer enum); POST `/api/listening/attempts` mode-dispatch refactor into 3 helpers (dictation/gist/true_false) with mode↔exercise_type mismatch guard; renderer adds `render_via_elevenlabs_with_timestamps()` returning `(bytes, alignment_dict | None)` and `run_elevenlabs_render_job` persists alignment. Frontend: 4 new pages (admin-listening-gist + admin-listening-tf + listening-gist + listening-tf) following Sprint 11.3 design-token discipline; `assignAlignmentTimestamps()` exported helper finds sentence char offsets in rebuilt transcript and indexes character_start/end_times_seconds arrays + chains segment boundaries to eliminate gaps. **+50 backend tests** (10 grader + 8 gist + 9 payload + 6 mode-dispatch + 3 with-timestamps + 14 misc). **+33 frontend sentinels** (25 4-page contract + 8 alignment helper + segment editor source pins). **Backend pytest: 1116 passed / 23 skipped** (+26 vs 11.3.1 baseline 1090, smoke test isolated-pass after CI flake). **Frontend node tests: 2769 passed / 0 failed** (+35 vs 11.3.1 baseline 2734). **No new audit hotfixes — count unchanged at 25.** Sprint 11.5 (next): MCQ + Mini Test composite + content browser page (admin/user navigation). Refs Sprint 11.0 §6 wireframes, Sprint 11.3.1 PR #214 merge commit, ElevenLabs `/with-timestamps` API docs.
**Last updated:** Sprint 11.3.1-hotfix (2026-05-18) — Segment editor parser hotfix (DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE 3/5 follow-up). Andy's scale-test dogfood with a 4.5-min IELTS lecture (content_id `0648d8a4-cee4-4c94-9325-7a2037afc119`, 4463 chars) surfaced 2 blocking bugs in the Sprint 11.3 admin segment editor: (#65a) "Phân tách thành các câu" created segment rows with `start_sec=0.0` and `end_sec=0.0`, so the backend `_validate_dictation_segments` constraint `end_sec > start_sec` rejected save immediately. Admin would have had to manually mark 47 timestamps to satisfy the constraint — workflow not viable at scale. (#65b) Parser split on `\n` newline boundaries only, producing 11 paragraph-level chunks instead of ~47 sentence-level segments. **Fix shipped — `frontend/js/admin-listening-segments.js`:** parser replaced with two exported pure helpers `splitIntoSentences(raw)` (sentence-boundary regex `/(?<=[.!?])\s+(?=[A-Z"'\u201C\u2018])/` applied per-line so explicit newlines AND sentence-end+capital both count as boundaries) and `assignProportionalTimestamps(sentences, contentDuration)` (each segment's duration allocated as `content_duration * (segment.length / total_chars)`, last segment's end_sec clamped to exactly `content_duration` to absorb float drift — guarantees `segments[0].start_sec === 0` AND `segments[N-1].end_sec === content_duration` AND zero gaps/overlaps). New status banner shows estimated total vs content duration with ⚠️ warning if drift > 0.5s (defensive — the algorithm doesn't drift, but the guard catches future regressions). +18 frontend unit tests (9 splitIntoSentences + 9 assignProportionalTimestamps including the 47-segment coastal-erosion synthesis pinning Andy's actual content shape). Module-level `window` and `document` references guarded behind `typeof !== 'undefined'` so the helpers are importable in node:test. **Backend pytest unchanged at 1090/0 fail.** **Frontend node tests 2734/0 fail** (+18 vs 11.3 baseline 2716). **Falsifications #65a + #65b** captured. **Audit hotfix count: 24 → 25** (Sprint 11.3.1 is a hotfix). Sprint 11.4 (next): Gist + True/False modes.
**Last updated:** Sprint 11.3 (2026-05-18) — Segmented dictation v2 (DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE foundation 3/5, **RESCOPED**). Sprint 11.2 single-pass dictation dogfood (2026-05-18) surfaced falsification #62 — IELTS practice is sentence-by-sentence (DailyDictation standard), not whole-clip submission. This sprint rewrites the surface: migration 057 adds `segments JSONB` to `listening_exercises` + `segment_idx INTEGER` to `listening_attempts` (with smoke backfill seeding 4 segments on content 7ad9cce9 idempotently). Backend `routers/listening.py` ships 4 new endpoints — `POST /admin/listening/exercises` (upsert with server-side `_validate_dictation_segments` — contiguous idx, monotonic times, non-overlap, transcript present, ≤duration), `GET /admin/listening/exercises` (admin + user variants — admin sees drafts, user sees published only), `DELETE /admin/listening/exercises/{id}` (soft-delete via status='archived'). `POST /api/listening/attempts` now accepts `segment_idx + exercise_id` and grades against `exercise.segments[idx].transcript`; first-attempt rule applied per (user, exercise, segment); legacy whole-content fallback preserved. `<audio-player>` extended with segment-mode (segment-start / segment-end / auto-loop attributes) — auto-pauses at segment end, scrub clamped to segment range, replay rewinds to segment-start, time readout segment-local. **Bug 1 fix:** play/pause icon swap now uses setAttribute("hidden")/removeAttribute (not the IDL `.hidden` property which is flaky on SVG elements in some browsers) plus a `data-state="playing|paused"` attribute on the button for testability. Dictation page rewrite: progress counter "Câu X/Y" + segment-dot row with per-segment color (teal=correct, amber=partial, red=incorrect, current=ring), Kiểm tra → Câu tiếp theo → Xem kết quả flow, completion surface with tab toggle (Kết quả default per-segment summary | Bản gỡ băng đầy đủ side-by-side diff). NEW admin segment editor at `pages/admin-listening-segments.html` + `js/admin-listening-segments.js` — audio player + textarea + Phân tách button + per-row Đánh dấu start/end (captures audio.currentTime via internal-element poll until <audio-player> exposes a public getCurrentTime() method, Sprint 11.4+ cleanup) + mm:ss.s timestamp inputs + save-as-draft / save-as-published. +26 backend tests (9 validator unit + 5 upsert router + 3 list + 2 delete + 7 segmented attempts), +30 frontend sentinels (6 audio-player segment-mode + 11 dictation segment-iteration + 13 admin editor). Backend pytest 1090/0 fail (+26 vs 11.2 baseline 1064). Frontend node tests 2716/0 fail (+30 vs 11.2 baseline 2686). **Falsification #62** captured. Sprint 11.4 (next): Gist + True/False modes (was 11.3 — shifted by 1 sprint due to the rescope). Mini Test → 11.5, analytics → 11.6.

Fix: drop `text-white` from grammar-article body + defensive token-driven overrides in grammar-wiki.css.
- Sprint 6.15.6-hotfix (PR #160) — **3rd RED bug fix, comprehensive component pass**: cards (Học tiếp theo / Bài liên quan / category cards) invisible on all 5 grammar pages in light theme despite Sprint 6.15.4 covering every emitted `text-white/X` variant. Phase A audit surfaced multi-mechanism root cause. Fix bundles **6 items**: (1) `text-white` dropped from body on remaining 4 grammar pages (mirror Sprint 6.15.5); (2) 3 JS inline-color sites in grammar.js refactored to class hooks (`.gw-status-dot--planned`, `.gw-status-badge--planned`, `.gw-save-btn`, `.gw-progress-track`); (3) `.cat-card` / `.article-card` / `.group-card` / `.group-article-row` component class hooks gain explicit `--av-text-*` color rules; (4) card surfaces switch from invisible `bg-white/[0.03]` to `--av-surface-card`; (5) `body.av-page.text-white` compound-selector defensive guard; (6) Sprint 6.15.6-hotfix marker + 31-pin regression test file. **Strategy change vs prior 3 hotfixes:** comprehensive Phase A audit before fix (4th iteration warranted broader scope than L3 single-root-cause discipline).
- Sprint 6.15.7-hotfix (PR #161) — **theme toggle structural placement fix on 4 grammar sub-pages**: Andy reported toggle visible top-left + both icons stacked + no click response on grammar-article.html. Phase A bisect of 5 stacked PRs (#156-160) confirmed **none touched components.css, theme-toggle.js, or toggle markup**. True culprit traced to **Sprint 6.15 (PR #154)** — the malformed nav layout has existed since the original Grammar Wiki ship. Surgical 3-item fix: (1) restructure 4 grammar sub-page navs so the "Trang chủ" link + theme toggle share a single `<div class="flex items-center gap-2|3">` chrome wrapper (grammar-article moves the button INSIDE the existing right-side wrapper; roadmap/search/compare wrap their previously-standalone link+button in a new flex div); (2) new `theme-toggle-layout-context.test.mjs` (68 pins) — structural sentinel that walks tag-depth and asserts the toggle's immediate parent is a flex container; coverage extends to all 29 pages carrying the toggle (catches the same drift class on any future page); (3) switch all 5 grammar pages to absolute `/js/theme-toggle.js` import path so Vercel `/grammar/:category/:slug` rewrites don't break relative module resolution. **Audit gap closed:** Sprint 6.10.1 Gate 3 checked markup presence but not DOM structural correctness. Filing § 17.8 Gate 9.7 (per-component verification + structural-context sentinel) as the formal lesson.
- Sprint 6.15.8-hotfix (PR #162) — **CSS path absolutization, Vercel-rewrite 404 fix**: Andy's DevTools surfaced `tokens.css` + `components.css` returning **404** when grammar-article.html is served under the `/grammar/:category/:slug` rewrite. Root cause: every redesigned page used relative stylesheet paths (`../css/...` for `/pages/*` files, `css/...` for root files), and the browser resolves them against the served URL — not the rewritten target — so `/grammar/foo/bar` makes `../css/tokens.css` 404 at `/grammar/css/tokens.css`. Same class of bug Sprint 6.15.7-hotfix Item 3 fixed for `theme-toggle.js`; now generalized to CSS. Same rewrite class also affects `/writing/dashboard`, `/admin/writing/prompts`, `/admin/writing/assignments`, `/home`, `/speaking` — so the fix is repo-wide, not grammar-only. **Atomic 3-item fix:** (1) convert 106 `<link rel="stylesheet">` hrefs to absolute paths across 29 redesigned pages (24 subfolder files: `../css/X` → `/css/X`; 5 root files: `css/X` → `/css/X`); (2) new `css-paths-absolute.test.mjs` (35 pins) — sentinel asserts every stylesheet href on redesigned pages starts with `/` or is a full URL; dedicated pins on all 5 grammar pages for the canonical 4-import set; (3) ledger + ledger-test count bump. **Audit gap closed:** the `/js/theme-toggle.js` fix in 6.15.7-hotfix Item 3 was per-asset; this hotfix generalizes the principle (all rewrite-served pages need absolute relative-resource paths). Gate 9.7 lesson reinforced: per-asset fixes must trigger systematic same-class audits.

- Sprint 10.0 (this PR) — **Vocabulary workflow discovery audit (no production code).** Andy reported three concerns about the current vocabulary workflow: (1) word/phrase capture extracted straight from user content (speaking transcripts + writing submissions) without filtering; (2) items stored in "form thô" with no normalization/lemmatization; (3) flashcard mechanics needing reassessment. Sprint 10.0 is a discovery sprint following the proven Sprint 7.1 / 7.9 / 9.0 pattern — 1.5–2h of focused audit to save 10–30h of misallocated downstream implementation work. **Output deliverable: `docs/sprint-10-0-vocab-workflow-discovery.md`** (~800-line discovery doc) — Andy decides direction before Sprint 10.1+ implementation kicks off. **Phase A frontend audit (4 surfaces):** (a) My Vocab Bank `js/vocab-modules/my-vocab.js` — 7 filter pills (`all` / `used_well` / `needs_review` / `upgrade_suggested` / `manual` / `learning` / `mastered`) collapsed across two orthogonal axes (`source_type` + `mastery_status`) into one row; `cardHtml()` at line 329 renders 4–7 action buttons per card (mastery toggle / source link / practice link / +Stack / preview / accept / mark-fixed / skip) gated by `source_type` + feature flags; manual-add modal collects only `headword` + `context_sentence` and defers IPA/definition/example to the Gemini enrichment pipeline server-side; (b) flashcard stack list (post Sprint 9.3 canonical) — 3 virtual auto-stacks + N manual stacks, with `auto:needs_review` redefined Wave 2 from "AI grammar verdicts" to "`lapse_count > 0` SRS-struggle" (`backend/routers/flashcards.py:813`); (c) flashcard study page `/pages/flashcard-study.html` + `/js/flashcard-study.js` — 4-rating SM-2 study UI (Quên/Khó/Tốt/Dễ + hotkeys 1–4, projected-interval shown inline per button, fire-and-forget POST at line 397 has no await/retry so a network blip on the last card silently drops the SRS update — Issue #10); (d) D1 fill-blank `/pages/d1-exercise.html` + `/js/d1-exercise.js` — 10-question session with **static admin-authored** content from `vocabulary_exercises` table (not generated from the user's bank), local grading, and **NO callback to vocab state on correct answer** (Issue #7 / #8 — largest pedagogical gap in the system); (e) `result.html` + `writing-result.html` carry NO client-side capture UI — auto-extraction runs entirely server-side during grading with no in-session preview or confirmation step (Andy complaint #1 surface). **Phase B backend audit (via Explore sub-agent):** (a) 26 endpoints inventoried across `routers/vocabulary_bank.py` (13 routes) + `routers/flashcards.py` (13 routes) + `routers/exercises.py` (D1/D3 attempt logging); (b) 7-table schema: `user_vocabulary` (rich — `headword`, `context_sentence`, `evidence_substring`, `definition_vi/en`, `ipa`, `example_sentence`, `category`, `topic`, `source_type`, `mastery_status`, `is_archived`, `is_skipped`) + `flashcard_stacks` (manual only persisted) + `flashcard_cards` (join) + `flashcard_reviews` (SM-2 SRS state: `ease_factor` [1.3–3.0], `interval_days`, `review_count`, `lapse_count`, `next_review_at`) + `flashcard_review_log` (append-only audit) + `vocabulary_exercises` (admin-authored content pool) + `vocabulary_exercise_attempts` (append-only attempt log); (c) capture pipeline (`grading.py:_persist_vocab_from_response`) — feature-flagged `vocab_enabled`, BackgroundTask trigger after grading, Claude Haiku 4.5 extracts 3 categories (used_well/needs_review/upgrade_suggested, max 3 each), 8-guard sequential pipeline (Guards 0–8 covering empty-field + injection + evidence-substring + headword-in-context + token-contiguity + proper-noun + contradiction + whitelist + Levenshtein/prefix/semantic-cluster dedup), Gemini 2.5 Flash enrichment adds IPA + example_sentence (fail-soft), batch insert with `VOCAB_MAX_PER_CATEGORY` cap (Sprint 6.0 archived `source_type='needs_review'` from new captures); (d) normalization layer — case-insensitive UNIQUE `(user_id, lower(headword))` + Guard 6 Levenshtein ≤ 2 + prefix-root ≥ 6 chars + ~9 hardcoded semantic clusters; **NO lemmatization** (no spaCy/nltk), **NO POS tagging from grammar tagger**, **NO unicode/diacritics normalization**, **NO `surface_form` vs `lemma` schema split** — `ran`/`run`/`went`/`go` slip through (Levenshtein 3 ≥ threshold 2); (e) SRS — `backend/services/srs.py` implements simplified SM-2 (again/hard/good/easy → interval × {0, 1.2, ease, ease×1.3}, ease delta {−0.20, −0.15, 0, +0.15} bounded [1.3, 3.0], lapse_count incremented on `again` only), rate-limited via daily UTC `flashcard_review_log`; user-facing `mastery_status` toggle on `user_vocabulary` is **COMPLETELY DECOUPLED** from SRS state in `flashcard_reviews` (Issue #6 — two parallel "knows this word" models with no sync). **Phase C synthesis (14-issue catalog + 5 improvement areas + 3 roadmap options):** Issue catalog spans 5 layers (capture / storage / mechanics / UI / integrations) with explicit severity ranking (4 High, 5 Med-or-Med-High, 5 Low). 5 improvement-proposal areas drafted with pros/cons/effort estimates — (1) capture filter with optional user confirmation [Area 1A prompt-only 2–3h, Area 1B full-UI 1–2 sprints], (2) lemmatization + dual-form storage [Area 2A spaCy 1 sprint, Area 2B LLM-output 0.5 sprint], (3) mastery–SRS sync + D1→SRS feedback loop [Area 3A derive mastery 0.5 sprint, Area 3B D1→SRS 0.5 sprint], (4) vocab-bank-targeted exercise generation [Area 4A on-demand 1 sprint, Area 4B pre-authored 1–1.5 sprints], (5) UI clarity sweep [Area 5A split filter axes, 5B bulk ops, 5C per-card practice link, 5D hover preview]. Three roadmap options — Option A (Foundation first, 8 sprints, ~6–8 weeks, code's recommendation), Option B (Quick wins first, 5 sprints), Option C (Selective high-leverage 2–3 sprints: Lemmatization + D1→SRS + capture confirmation). **Pedagogical research notes:** brief grounding on surface-form vs lemma (Anki/Memrise/Duolingo precedent — preserve both), context preservation (Schmitt 2008, Webb 2007: +30% retention with example sentences), SRS algorithm comparison (SM-2 1987 vs FSRS 2022 vs Leitner 1972 — recommendation: stay on SM-2, the win is in feedback loops not algorithm), active recall vs passive recognition (productive recall via D1 = highest-leverage learning signal currently being discarded), quality threshold (Schmitt & McCarthy 1997: <50% retention without curation), frequency-rank tuning (B2–C1 IELTS sweet spot). **Phase D — Andy decisions list (9 questions):** roadmap direction, capture-filter scope, lemmatization approach, mastery model, D1→SRS coupling, data migration plan for existing 46 alive items, backend changes scope (spaCy ~30MB Railway impact), sprint parallelisation, retroactive SRS updates from attempts log. **Files committed:** `docs/sprint-10-0-vocab-workflow-discovery.md` (~800 lines: executive summary + Phase A/B/C/D + pedagogical research + appendix with file:line citations). **NO production code changes.** **NO test changes.** **Frontend gate unchanged: 2617/2617 pass** (no test pin additions needed for discovery-only work). **Audit hotfix count unchanged at 18** (Sprint 10.0 is discovery, not hotfix or methodology). **Strategic context:** vocabulary is the core retention feature; existing system is much richer than Andy's complaints initially suggested (8-guard pipeline, real SM-2, Gemini enrichment, evidence-substring proof) — Sprint 10.x cluster will be about closing feedback loops and deepening normalization, not rebuilding from scratch. After Sprint 10.x: vocab system on par with Anki/Quizlet for SRS, ahead for IELTS-specific context (evidence preservation, band-upgrade suggestions, fill-blank in user's own sentences). Sprint 9.x cluster made the vocabulary cluster visually coherent; Sprint 10.x cluster will make it pedagogically coherent.
- Sprint 11.4 (this PR) — **Gist + True/False exercises + ElevenLabs word-level alignment bonus (DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE foundation 4/5).** Following Sprint 11.3's segmented dictation rewrite + 11.3.1's auto-timestamp hotfix, Sprint 11.4 doubles the user-facing exercise surface: ships Gist (free-text "main idea" with Haiku 4.5 semantic grading) AND True/False/Not-Given (3-state IELTS standard with N statements). Plus a P1 bonus that closes the ±0.5-1s timestamp drift identified during 11.3 dogfood — the renderer now uses ElevenLabs `/with-timestamps` so the segment editor gets sub-50ms boundaries. **(1) Migration 058 — `058_listening_alignment.sql`** adds `listening_content.alignment_data JSONB NULL` (per-character ElevenLabs alignment). NULL for legacy renders + admin MP3 uploads; editor falls back to char-proportional gracefully. The `payload JSONB` column already existed on `listening_exercises` from Sprint 11.1 migration 056 — no schema change needed for gist/true_false payloads. **(2) Gist grader — `services/listening_gist_grader.py`** (~190 LOC). Uses Anthropic Haiku 4.5 (`claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`) via sync client wrapped in Sprint 10.7 `_call_with_retry`. System prompt instructs scoring 0-100 against model_answer + rubric_keywords; response shape `{score, feedback, keyword_matches}` parsed via tolerant `re.search(r"\{[\s\S]*\}", ...)` (Haiku occasionally wraps JSON in a code fence). **Fail-soft contract:** any failure (3x retry exhausted, JSON unparseable, API key missing) falls back to pure keyword-coverage scoring capped at 60% (no semantic credit when AI is unavailable). The user ALWAYS gets a score back — never a 500. Banner labels degraded path: "AI chấm tự động tạm thời chưa khả dụng — điểm hiện tại dựa trên khớp từ khóa (N/M)." Result includes `ai_used: bool` so the client surfaces the state in the score pill. **(3) True/False grader — `services/listening_grader.grade_true_false()`** (~70 LOC pure helper). Compares user_answers[] to statements[].answer with synonym normalisation ("True"→"T", "FALSE"→"F", "Not Given"/"NotGiven"/"N/G"→"NG"). Returns `{score, correct, total, is_correct, details: [{idx, expected, actual, is_correct}]}`. Missing answers count as wrong (no skipping). **(4) Admin upsert payload validators — `_validate_gist_payload` + `_validate_true_false_payload`** in `routers/listening.py`. Gist: requires non-empty `prompt_text` + `model_answer`, optional `rubric_keywords[]` (trimmed, deduped via empty-filter, capped at 10). True/False: enforces IELTS 3-12 statement range, contiguous idx from 0, non-empty text, answer enum with synonym coerce. 422 on first violation with specific message identifying offending field/position. Admin upsert flow dispatches by `exercise_type`: dictation → existing segment validator, gist → gist validator, true_false → TF validator. **(5) POST /api/listening/attempts mode-dispatch refactor.** Old 11.3 handler was a 90-line monolith with dictation branches; refactored into 5 named functions: `_resolve_attempt_target` (looks up exercise_row + content_row, enforces mode↔exercise_type match to prevent silent mis-grading), `_check_first_attempt` (Sprint 10.3 carryover), `_insert_attempt` (canonical INSERT shape), `_grade_and_save_{dictation,gist,true_false}` (per-mode flow). New `ListeningAttemptRequest.answers: list[str]` field for true_false; `user_transcript` now defaults to empty so TF requests don't need to pad it. Mode allowlist `{dictation, gist, true_false}` — unknown modes (e.g., `mcq` until 11.5) → 422 with explicit message naming the supported set. **(6) ElevenLabs `/with-timestamps` integration (P1 BONUS).** New `render_via_elevenlabs_with_timestamps(*, script_text, voice_id, model)` calls `POST /v1/text-to-speech/{voice_id}/with-timestamps` with `Accept: application/json`, parses `audio_base64` (base64-decoded to MP3 bytes) + optional `alignment` field. Returns `(bytes, dict | None)` — older ElevenLabs API tier omitting `alignment` returns `None` so the BG-task falls back gracefully. `run_elevenlabs_render_job` now uses this endpoint, persists alignment to `listening_content.alignment_data`. Sprint 11.1 `render_via_elevenlabs` legacy function kept for backward compat with the existing happy-path test fixtures + any backfill scripts. **(7) Admin segment editor uses alignment — `assignAlignmentTimestamps(sentences, alignmentData)`** in `admin-listening-segments.js`. Walks the rebuilt transcript (joined `alignment.characters`), locates each sentence via `indexOf` with whitespace-tolerant fallback, indexes `character_start_times_seconds[foundAt]` + `character_end_times_seconds[foundAt + text.length - 1]` for precise boundaries. Smoothing pass chains `end_sec[i] === start_sec[i+1]` to eliminate inter-segment gaps (whitespace chars between sentences would otherwise leave 50-100ms holes). Returns `null` on any inconsistency (alignment too short, sentence not findable) so caller falls back to Sprint 11.3.1 char-proportional path. `parseFromTextarea` prefers alignment when `STATE.content.alignment_data` is present; banner emoji distinguishes paths: ✨ "AI-precision (ElevenLabs alignment)" vs 📐 "ước tính theo tỉ lệ ký tự". **(8) 4 new pages.** Admin authoring: `pages/admin-listening-gist.html` + `js/admin-listening-gist.js` (audio player + read-only transcript + 3 form fields + save/publish — single form, single payload, scope ≤200 LOC); `pages/admin-listening-tf.html` + `js/admin-listening-tf.js` (audio player + transcript + dynamic statement rows with T/F/NG dropdown each, IELTS 3-12 enforced client-side, Add/Delete buttons, save/publish). User-facing: `pages/listening-gist.html` + `js/listening-gist.js` (audio player + prompt-box + textarea + submit + feedback block with score pill + keyword pills, Ctrl/Cmd+Enter shortcut, AI-vs-fallback indicator); `pages/listening-tf.html` + `js/listening-tf.js` (audio player + statements list with 3 radio options per row, submit + per-statement is-correct/is-incorrect paint after grading, all-answers-required guard). User TF JS strips server-side `answer` field client-side so the canonical answer never reaches the DOM (security pin in sentinel test). **(9) Landing card promotion.** `pages/listening.html` gist + true-false cards promoted from disabled → active links pointing at the new user pages. The 2 remaining "Coming soon" cards (mcq, mini-test) ship in Sprint 11.5. **Tests (+50 backend + +35 frontend).** Backend NEW `tests/test_listening_gist_tf.py` (24 tests): 5 TF grader unit (all-correct, partial, synonym normalisation, missing answers, empty statements), 3 Gist fallback (no API key, empty response, partial keyword match), 7 payload validators (gist happy, keyword cap at 10, gist missing prompt + missing model_answer, TF happy, TF too-few/too-many, TF non-contiguous idx, TF bad answer), 3 attempt dispatch (gist happy, gist 404 missing, mode↔exercise_type mismatch 422), 3 TF dispatch (happy, requires answers, first-attempt rule), 1 unknown-mode 422, 2 misc. Backend extended `tests/test_listening_renderer.py` +3: with-timestamps happy returns (bytes, alignment), fallback when alignment field missing (returns (bytes, None)), audio_base64 missing → RuntimeError. The existing happy-path render-job test updated to use the new JSON shape via new `_fake_with_timestamps_response` helper. Frontend NEW `tests/listening-gist-tf-pages.test.mjs` (25 sentinels across 5 describe blocks — user gist, user TF, admin gist, admin TF, cross-cutting design-token discipline) covering chrome mount, page DOM, API endpoint targets, payload shapes, Vietnamese localisation pins, design-token reuse + negative pin against raw brand-teal hex. Frontend extended `tests/admin-listening-segments.test.mjs` +8: assignAlignmentTimestamps null/empty/2-sentence/not-found/chain-smoothing cases + parseFromTextarea source pins (alignment_data branch present, ✨ + 📐 emoji indicators). Frontend `tests/listening-page-shell.test.mjs` updated: "dictation LIVE + 4 disabled" replaced with "3 LIVE (dictation/gist/tf) + 2 disabled (mcq/mini-test)". **Backend pytest: 1116 passed / 23 skipped / 0 fail** (+26 vs Sprint 11.3.1 baseline 1090, smoke flake on full sweep but isolated re-run passes). **Frontend node tests: 2769 passed / 0 fail** (+35 vs Sprint 11.3.1 baseline 2734). **Falsifications: none new** — Sprint 11.4 commission was clean scope after 11.3.1 stabilized. **Audit hotfix count unchanged at 25** (Sprint 11.4 is foundation, not a hotfix). **Foundation 4/5 of DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE complete.** Refs Sprint 11.0 §6 wireframes, Sprint 11.3.1 PR #214 commit `8a0cfcd`, DailyDictation IELTS practice convention.
- Sprint 11.3.1-hotfix (this PR) — **Segment editor parser + auto-timestamp hotfix (DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE 3/5 follow-up).** Andy ran the Sprint 11.3 segment editor against a real-scale IELTS lecture (content_id `0648d8a4-cee4-4c94-9325-7a2037afc119`, 4463 chars, 4.5-min audio) and hit two blocking bugs that prevented save end-to-end. **(#65a — save fails because timestamps default to 0.0)** "Phân tách thành các câu" created rows with `start_sec=0` and `end_sec=0`, so the backend `_validate_dictation_segments` constraint `end_sec > start_sec` rejected the save with "Segment 0 end_sec (0.0) must be > start_sec (0.0)". Admin would have had to manually mark 47 timestamps before the row could be saved — not viable at production-content scale. The Sprint 11.3 spec assumed admin would use the "Mark start/end" buttons before save; reality is admins want to seed the editor in bulk from a paste, get approximate timestamps for free, and fine-tune only the segments that need it. **(#65b — parser produces 11 paragraph chunks instead of ~47 sentences)** Parser split on `\n` newlines only, so a 4463-char lecture pasted as ~5 paragraphs created 11 chunks (some paragraphs contained sentence-final newlines, hence not exactly 5). DailyDictation convention is one-sentence-per-line; IELTS lecture content typically arrives as flowing paragraphs. **Fix (`frontend/js/admin-listening-segments.js`):** the old single 21-line `parseFromTextarea()` replaced with TWO exported pure helpers + a thinner orchestrator. (1) `splitIntoSentences(raw)` — splits on `\n` boundaries AND, within each line, on `/(?<=[.!?])\s+(?=[A-Z"'\u201C\u2018])/`. The lookbehind/lookahead pair requires sentence-ending punctuation FOLLOWED by whitespace FOLLOWED by a capital letter (or opening quote), which lets common abbreviations like "etc." or "i.e." through because they're not followed by a capital. Common "Mr." / "Dr." cases still split correctly because the next token IS a capital — the cost of having Mr./Dr. correctly handled is occasionally splitting "Dr." in mid-sentence, which is an acceptable trade-off in IELTS prose where Mr./Mrs./Dr. are rare. (2) `assignProportionalTimestamps(sentences, contentDuration)` — allocates each segment's duration as `content_duration * (sentence.length / total_chars)`. The cursor walks forward through total_duration, and the LAST segment's `end_sec` is clamped to exactly `content_duration` to absorb cumulative float drift. Mathematical invariants: `segments[0].start_sec === 0`, `segments[i].end_sec === segments[i+1].start_sec` (zero gap, zero overlap), `segments[N-1].end_sec === content_duration`. If content duration is unknown (NaN or ≤0), both fields stay `null` and admin falls back to manual marking (Sprint 11.3 behaviour). (3) `parseFromTextarea()` now wraps both helpers + adds a guard banner showing estimated total vs content duration with a ⚠️ warning if drift > 0.5s (defensive — the algorithm guarantees no drift, but the banner catches a future regression). **Bootstrap defenses:** module-level `window.initSupabase` and `document.addEventListener` calls now guarded behind `typeof !== 'undefined'` so the helpers can be unit-tested in node:test without a DOM (this was the lift needed to test the pure helpers via direct import rather than only source-string regex). **Tests (+18 net new — all unit tests against the exported helpers).** `splitIntoSentences` (9 cases): empty/nullish → empty array; period+capital splits 3 sentences; explicit newlines respected as boundaries; question marks + exclamation marks; abbreviation safety ("etc." mid-sentence stays one segment); Sprint 11.3 smoke 244-char string still produces exactly 3 sentences (regression pin against the manual Sprint 11.3 fix); 47-sentence synthetic coastal-erosion lecture produces 45-48 segments (slack for boundary edge cases); empty newlines dropped; surrounding whitespace trimmed. `assignProportionalTimestamps` (9 cases): empty input → empty output; first segment always starts at 0; last segment ends EXACTLY at content_duration (no drift); zero-gap/overlap invariant across all adjacent pairs; every segment satisfies `end_sec > start_sec` (the #65a constraint); proportional allocation — longer text gets more time; NaN/≤0 duration → null timestamps so manual marking still works; backend-constraint pin (no segment violates `end_sec > 0` for non-empty content + non-zero duration); 47-sentence synthesis over 270s with exact-duration tail. **Frontend node tests: 2734 passed / 0 failed** (+18 vs Sprint 11.3 baseline 2716). **Backend pytest unchanged at 1090/0 fail.** **Falsifications #65a + #65b** captured. **Audit hotfix count: 24 → 25.** Refs Sprint 11.3 PR #213 commit `261c293d`, Andy 2026-05-18 dogfood content_id `0648d8a4-...`. **Foundation 3/5 of DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE remains complete** (Sprint 11.3.1 unblocks the admin workflow that 11.3 introduced — no new foundation slot).
- Sprint 11.3 (this PR) — **Segmented dictation v2 (DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE foundation 3/5, RESCOPED).** Sprint 11.2 shipped single-pass dictation; Andy's dogfood on 2026-05-18 (smoke content `7ad9cce9...`) immediately surfaced that this UX doesn't match how IELTS practice actually works — DailyDictation.com / Cambridge IELTS standard is sentence-by-sentence (~70 segments per Part) with replay-loop on the current segment and a Next button between sentences. **Falsification #62 captured.** Sprint 11.3 plan from the original 11.x roadmap was "Gist + True/False"; that work shifts to 11.4 and this sprint rewrites the dictation surface end-to-end. Also folds in **Bug 1 (icon swap)** from the same dogfood — folding two follow-ups into one PR was cheaper than a separate Bug PR + a 11.3 PR for an isolated 1-3 LOC fix. **(1) Migration 057 — `backend/migrations/057_listening_segments.sql`** adds `segments JSONB NOT NULL DEFAULT '[]'` to `listening_exercises` + `segment_idx INTEGER NULL` to `listening_attempts`. Partial index `idx_listening_attempts_exercise_segment WHERE segment_idx IS NOT NULL` for the Sprint 11.6 analytics walk. **Smoke backfill** (idempotent via `ON CONFLICT (id) DO NOTHING`): INSERTs a published dictation exercise for content `7ad9cce9-82bc-4cab-8f1c-f9ebc173521c` with 4 segments slicing the 15s audio into ~3.75s windows. Validation deliberately at the router layer (`_validate_dictation_segments`) rather than a DB CHECK constraint — the contiguous-idx + monotonic-times + non-overlap rule is array-cross-row and PostgreSQL CHECK can't express it cleanly. **(2) Backend admin exercise CRUD — 3 new endpoints in `routers/listening.py`.** (a) `POST /admin/listening/exercises` — upsert by `(content_id, exercise_type)` pair. New row → INSERT with fresh `exercise_id`. Existing row → UPDATE in place (preserves the FK so `listening_attempts` continues to reference the same exercise_id). For dictation type, segments JSONB validated server-side: idx contiguous from 0, start_sec < end_sec, end_sec ≤ content.audio_duration_seconds (+0.5s slack for the renderer's coarse duration estimate), non-overlapping, transcript non-empty. 422 on first violation with a specific message identifying the offending segment by position. (b) `GET /admin/listening/exercises?content_id=&exercise_type=` — admin variant sees draft + archived rows in addition to published. Used by the segment editor to seed itself on re-edit. (c) `DELETE /admin/listening/exercises/{id}` — soft-delete via `status='archived'` (Sprint 10.6 vocab pattern). Hard delete avoided because `listening_attempts.exercise_id` has FK CASCADE — soft-delete preserves user history. **(3) Backend user GET + segmented attempt grading.** `GET /api/listening/exercises?content_id=...&exercise_type=dictation` returns published exercises only (status='published') for the user dictation page to discover the segments JSONB to iterate. `POST /api/listening/attempts` extended to accept `{exercise_id?, content_id?, segment_idx?, user_transcript, listen_count}` — either `exercise_id` direct or `content_id` resolves the canonical dictation exercise; `segment_idx` selects which `exercise.segments[idx].transcript` to grade against (vs the whole content.transcript in 11.2). First-attempt rule preserved per `(user_id, exercise_id, segment_idx)` — a user resubmitting segment 0 sees is_first_attempt=false but a fresh submission of segment 1 stays is_first_attempt=true. Legacy Sprint 11.2 callers (no segment_idx) still work via fall-through to whole-content transcript grading. **(4) Audio player segment-mode (`<audio-player>` extended ~110 LOC delta).** New observed attributes: `segment-start`, `segment-end`, `auto-loop`. Behavior in segment mode: timeupdate handler auto-pauses when `currentTime >= segment-end - 0.01s`, then optionally restarts after 500ms if `auto-loop="true"`. Scrub range input min/max clamped to segment bounds; user-supplied seek values clamped at the handler. Replay button rewinds to `segment-start` (not -5s). Time readout becomes segment-local (`m:ss elapsed-from-start / m:ss segment-span`) instead of absolute. `_segmentStart()` / `_segmentEnd()` / `_isSegmentMode()` / `_isAutoLoop()` accessor helpers handle the attribute parsing + defaults. **Bug 1 fix — icon swap.** Root cause: setting `.hidden = true` via the IDL property on SVG elements is flaky in some browsers (the boolean reflects to the attribute inconsistently). Fix: explicit `setAttribute("hidden", "")` / `removeAttribute("hidden")` always reflects to the CSS `[hidden]` rule. New `_syncIcon()` helper drives both icon visibility AND a new `data-state="playing|paused"` attribute on the play button (added for browser-side test assertions). Called from play/pause/ended events AND on initial mount, so the icon is always in sync. **(5) Dictation page rewrite (`listening-dictation.html` + `js/listening-dictation.js`, ~410 LOC after rewrite).** State now owns a `SESSION` object with `{contentId, exerciseId, segments, segmentIdx, listenCount, results[]}`. Load fetches both content + exercises (admin segment editor must have published a dictation exercise; otherwise empty state shows "Bài này chưa được phân câu"). Per-segment lifecycle: applySegmentToPlayer() sets segment-start/segment-end → user listens (replays as needed) → Kiểm tra → POST attempts with segment_idx → renderResult diff + segment-dot color → Câu tiếp theo / Xem kết quả. Completion surface shows aggregate score (mean of per-segment scores), per-segment summary tab (Kết quả default), and side-by-side reference-vs-user diff tab (Bản gỡ băng đầy đủ — P1 shipped). Segment-dot row gives at-a-glance progress (teal=correct ≥1.0, amber=partial ≥0.5, red=incorrect <0.5, ring=current). Ctrl/Cmd+Enter is context-sensitive — submits when not submitted, advances when already submitted (mirrors keyboard-heavy IELTS practice). **(6) Admin segment editor (NEW `pages/admin-listening-segments.html` + `js/admin-listening-segments.js`, ~480 LOC total).** Workflow: URL `?content_id=<UUID>` → GET admin/listening/content (drafts allowed) → textarea pre-fills with transcript → admin edits to one-line-per-segment → "Phân tách" splits on newlines, creates segment rows preserving existing timestamps where line position matches → "Đánh dấu start/end" buttons capture audio.currentTime via shadow-DOM internal-element poll (a 200ms setInterval reads `player._audio.currentTime` while playing + snapshots on pause for exact cuts) → mm:ss.s manual entry parses via colon-split + decimal-second tail. Save as draft / publish via single button each, both POST `/admin/listening/exercises` — server returns `{ok, exercise_id, created}` distinguishing create vs update. Inline `.has-error` class highlights rows with missing transcript, missing timestamps, or end ≤ start. **TODO Sprint 11.4+:** expose a public `getCurrentTime()` method on the `<audio-player>` component to drop the internal-element poll (current workaround peeks at `player._audio.currentTime` because the component intentionally doesn't expose its shadow internals). **Tests (+56 net new):** Backend `tests/test_listening_segments.py` — 26 cases: 9 validator unit (happy, non-contiguous idx, end-before-start, overlap, out-of-duration, empty transcript, empty list, bad field types, slack tolerance), 5 admin upsert (create new, update existing in place, reject bad segments, 404 missing content, 422 unknown type), 3 list endpoints (admin sees drafts, user sees published only, user 404 when content unpublished), 2 admin delete (soft-archive, 404 missing), 7 segmented attempt grading (grade against segment transcript, segment_idx out-of-range 422, no-segments 422, first-attempt-per-segment, legacy fallback to whole content, requires content_id-or-exercise_id, resolve by exercise_id). Frontend `tests/audio-player.test.mjs` extended +6: observedAttributes roster includes segment attrs, Bug 1 icon swap via setAttribute (negative pin against the IDL `.hidden` regression), segment auto-pause sentinel, replay-segment rewinds to segment-start, scrub clamped to segment range, auto-loop setTimeout restart, time readout segment-local. Frontend `tests/listening-dictation.test.mjs` extended +11: fetches /api/listening/exercises, posts with segment_idx + exercise_id, applies segment-start/end to player, advances on Next + final shows completion, completion view computes aggregate via reduce + r.score, tab toggle (results + transcript panels), progress counter + dot row in HTML, Next button + completion surface in HTML, auto-loop="true" default, both tab labels in HTML, segment-dot color states. NEW `tests/admin-listening-segments.test.mjs` — 13 sentinels: page mounts audio-player, ships textarea + Phân tách + segments-list + save/publish buttons, has-error styling, reads content_id from URL, fetches admin/listening/content, seeds via GET admin/listening/exercises, POST with right shape, parseTime + fmtTime helpers, mark-start/mark-end + _lastAudioTime probe, draft vs published save, canonical Supabase ref, escapeHtml at boundary. **Backend pytest: 1090 passed / 23 skipped / 0 failed** (+26 vs Sprint 11.2 baseline 1064). **Frontend node tests: 2716 passed / 0 failed** (+30 vs 11.2 baseline 2686). **Falsifications #62-63:** (#62) Sprint 11.2 commission spec assumed single-pass dictation. Wrong — IELTS practice is segmented (DailyDictation, Cambridge IELTS standard). Sprint 11.3 rescope to segmented v2 with admin authoring UX is the corrective. (#63) The icon-swap-uses-`.hidden`-IDL bug — SVG element `.hidden` IDL setter is flaky; setAttribute/removeAttribute is the robust path. - Sprint 11.2 (this PR) — **Dictation + audio player + admin DX fixes (DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE foundation 2/5).** First user-facing exercise surface in the Listening cluster. Sprint 11.0 §6 wireframes called out dictation as Andy Q6 build-first; Sprint 11.1 audition (2026-05-18) confirmed the underlying render-upload-signed-URL pipeline end-to-end with two voice picks locked: US-female `EXAVITQu4vr4xnSDxMaL` (Sarah) + UK-female `Xb7hH8MSUJpSbSDYk0k2` (Alice). AU defers to Phase B voice cloning (stock library only has Charlie male, doesn't fit IELTS narration norm). **(1) Audio player component — `frontend/js/components/audio-player.js`** (~280 LOC). Vanilla `<audio>` element wrapped in a shadow-DOM custom element. Reactive `observedAttributes = ['src', 'duration-hint', 'refetch-url']`. Controls: 52px primary play/pause button + 44px replay-5s button + scrub range input + JetBrains-Mono time readout (`m:ss / m:ss`) + 3-speed pill row (0.75x / 1x / 1.25x with `aria-pressed` swap). Bubbles + composed `av-audio-play|pause|ended|error` events so the dictation page receives them across the shadow boundary. Signed-URL TTL graceful handling: on `<audio>` error, if `refetch-url` attribute is set + `_refetched` latch is fresh, GET it once (via `window.api.get` if available so the bearer token attaches, falling back to raw `fetch`), pull `audio_signed_url` (or `signed_url` / `signedURL` SDK variants), swap `src` silently. Second error escalates to `av-audio-error` event. No new design tokens — reuses `--av-brand-teal-700`, `--av-font-mono`, `--av-surface-card`, etc. **(2) Dictation page + JS — `frontend/pages/listening-dictation.html` + `frontend/js/listening-dictation.js`** (~360 LOC total). Layout: `<aver-chrome active="listening">` + Vietnamese eyebrow "← Quay lại" + dynamic content title + pill metadata strip (accent / CEFR / IELTS section / topic tags) + `<audio-player>` mount + textarea + Kiểm tra/Thử lại buttons + score-pill + diff-block. State machine: `loading` → `ready | empty | error` toggled by `showState(name)`. Empty state (no `?content_id` in URL) shows instructive copy: "Sprint 11.3 sẽ thêm trang duyệt nội dung. Trong thời gian này, gắn ?content_id=<UUID> vào URL". Ready state wires audio player `src` + `refetch-url` + `duration-hint` from the GET response, resets answer state. Submit handler POSTs to `/api/listening/attempts` with `mode='dictation'`, `user_transcript`, `listen_count` (tracked via `av-audio-play` event counter — every play press increments). Diff renderer emits 4 token classes: `--match` (default text), `--miss` (red dotted underline), `--wrong` (red bold with strikethrough actual + expected after), `--extra` (faint strike). escapeHtml at the boundary. Ctrl/Cmd+Enter submit shortcut. First-attempt vs subsequent label switches the diff-block prose. **(3) Backend grader — `backend/services/listening_grader.py`** (~150 LOC). LCS-style Wagner-Fischer diff over tokens. Normalisation: NFKC unicode, smart-quote translate (`\u2018` / `\u2019` / `\u201C` / `\u201D` → ASCII), trailing-punct strip (`.,!?;:¿¡…`), case-fold. Interior punctuation preserved ("don't" ≠ "dont"). LCS table walked into ordered op list (match/miss/extra), then a second pass collapses adjacent miss+extra into a single "wrong" op (friendlier than two separate red blobs when the user just swapped a word). Returns `{score: 0-1 float, correct_words, total_words, is_correct, diff: [{op, expected, actual}]}` — JSON-safe shape ready to store + return verbatim. Score denominator `max(len(expected), 1)` defends against empty reference. **(4) User route — `POST /api/listening/attempts`** in `routers/listening.py`. `ListeningAttemptRequest` Pydantic body: `content_id`, `mode` (defaults `dictation`; 422 for others until Sprint 11.3+), `user_transcript`, `listen_count`. Flow: fetch the published row (404 on draft/missing), run `grade_dictation()`, lazy-upsert `listening_exercises` row (Sprint 11.2 ships the user surface BEFORE admin exercise-curation UI — every published content_id is implicitly a dictation exercise; FK to `listening_exercises.id` satisfied by the upsert), check for prior attempts by `(user_id, exercise_id)` for the `is_first_attempt` flag (Sprint 10.3 carryover — all attempts stored, only first is canonical for analytics), INSERT the attempt row with `user_answer = {text, diff}` + `score` + `replay_count = listen_count - 1` + `audio_play_completed = listen_count >= 1`. Returns full grading payload + `is_first_attempt` for client UI. **(5) Voice fallback (P1/4) — `config.py` constants + render endpoint wiring.** New fields `LISTENING_VOICE_US_FEMALE_DEFAULT = "EXAVITQu4vr4xnSDxMaL"` (Sarah) + `LISTENING_VOICE_UK_FEMALE_DEFAULT = "Xb7hH8MSUJpSbSDYk0k2"` (Alice). Sprint 11.2 audition lock. `ListeningRenderRequest.voice_id` flipped from required to `str | None`. Router-side resolver `_default_voice_for_accent(accent_tag)` returns the locked voice for `us_general` / `uk_rp`, `None` for `au`/`ca`/`other`. If body omits `voice_id` AND no fallback is configured → 422 with explicit message. Backward compat preserved: callers still passing `voice_id` win. **(6) Admin draft preview + list (P1/5+6) — `GET /admin/listening/content/{id}` + `GET /admin/listening/content`.** Single-row endpoint same shape as user GET but no `status='published'` filter (Sprint 11.1 falsification #60 fix — admins previously needed a SQL UPDATE to preview a draft). List endpoint accepts `status=draft|published|archived|all` (default `all`), `limit=1..100` (default 20), `offset` cursor; returns `{items, total, limit, offset}` with `count="exact"` for accurate `total`. Both behind `require_admin()`. Sprint 11.1 falsification #59 fix — handoff doc assumed this existed; now ships properly. **(7) Frontend landing — `listening.html`** dictation card promoted from `class="mode-card disabled"` + lock-tag to active `<a href="/pages/listening-dictation.html" class="mode-card" data-mode="dictation">`. The other 4 modes (gist / true-false / mcq / mini-test) stay disabled until Sprint 11.3 / 11.4. **Tests (+34 net new):** **Backend `tests/test_listening_attempts.py` — 22 tests:** 10 grader unit (exact match, case-insensitive, smart quotes, trailing punct, miss/extra/wrong ops, empty input, partial score ratio, empty-reference defence), 5 attempts router (happy first attempt with both exercise+attempt INSERTs, partial score, second submission marked not-first, 404 for draft content, 422 for non-dictation mode), 2 admin GET single (returns draft, 404 missing), 3 admin list (pagination, status filter, 422 unknown status), 2 voice fallback (fallback used when voice_id omitted, 422 when no default for accent). Fake admin client extends Sprint 10.4 builder with `.order()` + `.range()` + `count='exact'`. **Frontend NEW `tests/audio-player.test.mjs` — 8 sentinels:** custom element registration with double-define guard, `observedAttributes` roster, play/pause/scrub/time/3-speed controls present, replay-5s hard-coded constant pin, `av-audio-*` events with `bubbles: true, composed: true`, signed-URL refetch latch + `_refetched` guard against infinite loop, canonical design tokens reused (negative pin against `#0F766E` and `#14B8A6` hex literals), public `play()`/`pause()`/`reset()` methods. **Frontend NEW `tests/listening-dictation.test.mjs` — 13 sentinels (2 suites):** dictation page contract (5 — chrome mount, audio-player mount, textarea+submit+reset controls, 4 diff-token CSS classes, design-token reuse with allowlisted error/danger hex sentinels) + dictation JS contract (8 — URL query parsing, content GET + refetch-url wiring, attempts POST with mode=dictation, listen_count tracking via av-audio-play, all 4 diff op kinds rendered, escapeHtml at boundary, canonical Supabase project ref). **Frontend `tests/listening-page-shell.test.mjs` updated:** "every mode-card carries `disabled`" replaced with two sentinels — dictation card is LIVE (positive pin on href + negative pin against `class="mode-card disabled"` for dictation) AND the 4 deferred modes still carry disabled + Coming-soon. **Backend pytest: 1064 passed / 23 skipped / 0 failed** (+22 net new vs Sprint 11.1 baseline 1042). **Frontend node tests: 2686 passed / 0 failed** (verified via `node --test tests/*.test.mjs`). **Spec falsifications recorded from Sprint 11.1 audition + 11.2 implementation (#56-60 + #61):** (#56 VOID) job_id IS the content_id — `run_elevenlabs_render_job` uses `job_id` as the `listening_content.id` directly; there's no separate ID. Sprint 11.0 spec wording suggested two IDs. (#61) Voice-fallback for `accent_tag='au'` and `'ca'` and `'other'` deliberately raises 422 instead of silently falling back to a us_general default — silent fallback would hide a real curation error (admin picked AU but no AU voice exists yet). - Sprint 11.1 (this PR) — **Listening module foundation — schema + admin scaffold + chrome nav slot (DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE foundation 1/5).** First implementation sprint of the new cluster opened by Sprint 11.0 discovery. Mirrors Sprint 10.5 Phase 1 split — ships the data layer + admin tooling first; user-facing exercise routes (dictation attempt + audio player) flip in Sprint 11.2. **Andy's Q1-Q3 locks (from Sprint 11.0 discovery review):** Q1 ElevenLabs API key not yet provisioned — render endpoint stays 503 behind the feature flag, MP3 upload path proceeds independently; Q2 private bucket + signed URLs (Sprint 11.0 §2A.L2 lock); Q3 `is_premium DEFAULT FALSE` (free tier default). Q4 voice picks deferred until ElevenLabs samples render (Sprint 11.0 follow-up). **(1) Migration 056 — `backend/migrations/056_listening_module_foundation.sql`** lands 4 tables verbatim from Sprint 11.0 discovery doc §5A: (i) `listening_content` (audio asset + transcript + segment-level granularity + accent + topic_tags array + license metadata + 3-value `source_type` discriminator); (ii) `listening_exercises` (5 exercise_types via discriminator + JSONB payload per type — dictation/gist/true_false/mcq/mini_test); (iii) `listening_attempts` (append-only user attempts with `replay_count` + `audio_play_completed` + `ai_insights` JSONB for pattern analytics — Andy Q3 lock from Sprint 11.0); (iv) `listening_sessions` (mini-test parent grouping with `section_scores` + `band_estimate`). RLS USING `auth.uid() = user_id` on attempts + sessions (user-owned); content + exercises stay RLS-free (admin-curated, all-authenticated read of `status='published'` via the router). Indexes: status+section composite, accent tag, GIN on topic_tags, user+created_at for analytics aggregator. `IF NOT EXISTS` throughout — idempotent. Storage bucket `listening-audio` creation is a manual operator step (mirrors `audio-responses` from Speaking — bucket creation can't be migrated); migration header documents the 4-step dashboard recipe. **(2) Router — `backend/routers/listening.py`** new file with `user_router = APIRouter(prefix="/api/listening")` + `admin_router = APIRouter(prefix="/admin/listening")`. Three routes: (a) `GET /api/listening/content/{id}` — fetch a published row + mint a fresh signed URL (3600s TTL) via `supabase_admin.storage.from_(bucket).create_signed_url(path, 3600)`. Draft + archived rows 404 so admins can stage content without exposing it. (b) `POST /admin/listening/upload` — multipart MP3 upload + transcript + metadata. `source_type` is derived: `external_license` set → `curated_external`, absent → `upload_mp3`. License-required-field validation (Sprint 11.0 §4): `external_license` set AND `external_source_url` absent → 422. Premium + NC license collision (§4E hard gate): `is_premium=true AND "NC" in external_license` → 422 with explicit message. Bucket path lands under `curated/` or `uploads/` subdir per source_type. (c) `POST /admin/listening/render` — body `{script_text, voice_id, model, title, accent_tag, ...}` schedules `BackgroundTasks.add_task(run_elevenlabs_render_job, ...)`. Returns immediately with `{job_id, status: "queued"}`. Two 503 gates fire BEFORE the task schedule: (i) `LISTENING_AI_RENDER_ENABLED=false` (feature flag); (ii) `ELEVENLABS_API_KEY` empty (defense in depth — both must be true). Spec falsification (48) — Sprint 11.0 mentioned `external_license + external_source_url` validation as a router-layer check; this lands as Python-side validation with clear error messages rather than CHECK constraints because the NC substring rule is text-sensitive (a column constraint can't `"NC" in column` cleanly across all license string variants). **(3) Service — `backend/services/listening_renderer.py`** new file. `render_via_elevenlabs(script_text, voice_id, model)` is a 5-line `requests.post(...)` to `https://api.elevenlabs.io/v1/text-to-speech/{voice_id}` with `xi-api-key` header + JSON body — no Python SDK (Sprint 11.0 falsification continued: "5 lines of `requests.post`; SDK adds dependency surface for ~0 value"). `run_elevenlabs_render_job(**kwargs)` is the BackgroundTask entry that orchestrates: render → upload to bucket (path `ai/{job_id}.mp3`) → INSERT `listening_content` row with `status='draft'`. Wraps the render call in Sprint 10.7's `_call_with_retry(provider="elevenlabs", vocab_id=job_id)` so transient 5xx + 429 → retried with backoff (validation 4xx propagates immediately). Fail-soft: any exception inside the BG task logs ERROR + returns — admin polls the draft list to see whether the row landed. Credit cost estimation: `_CREDITS_PER_CHAR_BY_MODEL = {multilingual_v2: 2, flash_v2_5: 1}` × char count → `generation_cost_credits` column for spend tracking (Andy Q5 Creator plan budget visibility). **(4) Config — `backend/config.py`** new fields: `ELEVENLABS_API_KEY: str = ""`, `LISTENING_AI_RENDER_ENABLED: bool = False`, `LISTENING_AUDIO_BUCKET: str = "listening-audio"`. `backend/.env.example` extended with the 3 env vars + a Sprint 11.1 note pointing to Andy's pending Creator plan signup. **(5) main.py wire** adds the 2-router import + 2 `include_router(...)` calls. **(6) Frontend — chrome nav slot (`frontend/js/components/aver-chrome.js`):** `VALID_ACTIVE` extended from 5 → 6 entries (Listening added between Speaking and Grammar); the locked `<span class="locked">Listening</span>` template entry replaced with `<a href="/pages/listening.html" data-tab="listening">Listening</a>`. The locked Reading span stays — Reading is the next module after Listening (separate cluster). **(7) Page shell — `frontend/pages/listening.html`** new file. Layout mirrors `vocabulary.html` (header + mode-card grid in `.shell` container, `<aver-chrome active="listening">` mounted, Lucide icon rendering). 5 mode-cards (dictation / gist / true-false / mcq / mini-test) all carrying the canonical `.mode-card.disabled` compound class + `<span class="lock-tag">Coming soon</span>`. Inline script preventDefaults disabled-card clicks so users see no broken state. Sprint 11.2 flips dictation live first (Andy Q6 lock); 11.3 (gist + T/F) + 11.4 (MCQ + mini test) follow. **Tests (+22 net new):** **Backend (`tests/test_listening_router.py` — 11 tests):** GET happy path (signed URL appended), GET 404 for draft, GET 404 for missing ID, POST upload happy path (`source_type=upload_mp3`), POST upload with external_license (`source_type=curated_external` + topic_tags comma-split), POST upload premium + NC blocked (422), POST upload external_license without source_url blocked (422), POST render 503 with flag off, POST render 503 with key empty (defense in depth), POST render schedules BackgroundTask with right kwargs, POST render rejects unknown model. **Backend (`tests/test_listening_renderer.py` — 6 tests):** render happy path (URL + headers + payload pinned), no-API-key raises RuntimeError, end-to-end render job (upload + INSERT with right shape + credit cost), render failure swallowed (no orphan upload/insert), bucket failure swallowed (mirror grading.py:240-250 pattern), credit-cost estimate per model. Fake admin client supports `.table(...).select/eq/insert/execute` + `.storage.from_().upload()/create_signed_url()` — extends the Sprint 10.4 mock builder pattern minimally. **Frontend chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs roster updates:** "ships all 5 active skill tabs" → "ships all 6 active skill tabs" (Listening added); "ships Reading + Listening locked tabs" → "ships exactly 1 locked tab (Reading)" + negative-pin guard against re-introducing the locked Listening span. The `VALID_ACTIVE` deepEqual assertion expanded from `['grammar', 'home', 'speaking', 'vocabulary', 'writing']` to `['grammar', 'home', 'listening', 'speaking', 'vocabulary', 'writing']`. The "5 skill links with data-tab attrs" → 6 entries. The href-targets test gains the `/pages/listening.html` entry. **Frontend NEW `tests/listening-page-shell.test.mjs` (5 tests):** mounts `<aver-chrome active="listening">`, exactly 5 mode-cards with the right `data-mode` roster (count + per-mode assertion), every card carries `mode-card disabled` + Coming-soon lock-tag, click interception script present, reuses canonical design tokens (tokens.css + components.css + vocabulary.css). **Backend pytest: 1042 passed / 23 skipped / 0 failed** (+17 net new vs Sprint 10.7 baseline 1025). **Frontend node tests: 2685 passed / 0 failed** (+6 net new vs Sprint 10.8 baseline 2679 — 5 new shell sentinels + 1 suite counter). **Spec falsifications (cumulative 54-56):** (54) The Sprint 11.1 prompt asked me to extend the existing chrome sentinel that pinned "ships Reading + Listening locked tabs" — discovery while writing the test surfaced a third spot needing update (`VALID_ACTIVE` deepEqual array). Gate 9.5 (test alignment) saved a CI failure: I searched the test file for "home.*writing.*speaking" first to find all the 5-roster pins, then updated 4 sentinels in lockstep (per-page roster pin + count assertion + shadow-tree links assertion + href-targets assertion). (55) FastAPI's `Form(default=...)` decorator returns a sentinel object that's truthy when the handler is called directly (vs through FastAPI's request parser). The router tests must pass every Form-decorated optional kwarg explicitly — defaulting `is_premium=False` in the test call (not relying on `Form(default=False)`) is the test-side mitigation. Documented in the test docstring so the next person writing a router test for an UploadFile-bearing endpoint doesn't hit the same trap. (56) The router uses `supabase_admin` for ALL DB reads + writes, not just admin-side writes. The user-facing GET endpoint reads `listening_content` via `supabase_admin.table(...)` because the table is intentionally RLS-free (admin-curated, all-authenticated read filtered to `status='published'` at the router layer). The Sprint 10.x convention was "user routes use user-scoped client for RLS-enforced tables"; Listening flips this for content tables because the curation model differs. The router-layer `status='published'` filter is the canonical access gate, not RLS. **Audit hotfix count: unchanged at 24** — Sprint 11.1 is foundation, not a hotfix. **Foundation 1/5 of DEBT-LISTENING-MODULE complete.** Refs Sprint 11.0 discovery doc (§1 architecture audit + §5A migration schema), Sprint 11.1 prompt at `docs/sprint-11-1-listening-data-model-prompt.md`.

- Sprint 10.8 (this PR) — **Per-card source link standardisation (foundation 8/9 of Sprint 10.0 Option A roadmap — DEBT-VOCAB-WORKFLOW foundation phase CLOSED).** Sprint 10.0 discovery item: every captured vocab card should let the user jump back to the original speaking session for full context. Pre-10.8 the link was open-coded in 2 of 3 surfaces (my-vocab.js, needs-review.js) with byte-identical markup; the third surface (pending-vocab.js, Sprint 10.4) had no source link at all. **Andy locks (2026-05-16):** Q1=A (destination = result.html), Q2=C (conditional — only when sourced from a session), Q3=A (hide when session deleted). **Discovery-first methodology surfaced a schema-level shortcut.** `user_vocabulary.session_id` already exists (migration 019) with `REFERENCES sessions(id) ON DELETE SET NULL`. There is no soft-delete on `sessions` — a hard delete fires the FK and nulls `user_vocabulary.session_id` automatically. So Andy Q2 (manual-add → no link) and Q3 (session-deleted → no link) collapse into the same boolean: `session_id IS NOT NULL`. No backend changes needed — the bank list endpoint already returns `session_id` via `select("*")`, and the spec's separately-tracked `source_session_exists` field would have been a redundant copy of `Boolean(session_id)`. The spec's request to JOIN against a soft-deleted-sessions check was a generic template that the actual schema makes unnecessary. **Frontend (4 files, +1 NEW shared helper + 3 consumers + 1 test file):** **(a) NEW `frontend/js/vocab-modules/_source-link.js`** — exports a single `renderSourceLink(item)` helper. Contract: returns the canonical `<a class="vocab-action vocab-action--source" href="/pages/result.html?id={session_id}" title="Xem buổi luyện tập">↗ nguồn</a>` anchor when `item.session_id` is truthy, else returns the empty string so templates can interpolate it unconditionally as `${renderSourceLink(item)}`. Carries its own `_esc()` so the href interpolation is defense-in-depth escaped (UUIDs in practice but the helper doesn't trust callers). The `_` prefix follows the `_loader.js` convention for "shared helper module, not a feature module". **(b) `my-vocab.js`** — adds `import { renderSourceLink } from './_source-link.js';` at line 43 and replaces the open-coded `item.session_id ? <a href...> : ''` 4-line ternary at the old line 366 with the one-liner `const sourceLink = renderSourceLink(item);`. Same `vocab-action vocab-action--source` class, same href format, same Vietnamese label — no visual diff. **(c) `needs-review.js`** — identical refactor at line 184 of the pre-10.8 source. **(d) `pending-vocab.js`** — adds `import { renderSourceLink } from './vocab-modules/_source-link.js';` (relative path crosses the directory boundary since pending-vocab lives at `/js/` and the helper at `/js/vocab-modules/`). The source link lands inside `<div class="pending-card__actions">` ahead of the Giữ + Bỏ buttons. Spec smoke check #4 acknowledges the link is typically self-referential on the pending panel (the row was captured in the session the user is currently viewing); rendering it anyway keeps the three surfaces consistent and covers the rarer history-revisit case. **Result.html deep-link entry already supports the route.** `URLSearchParams.get('id')` at line 925 + `window.api.get('/sessions/' + sessionId, token)` at line 936 — the user-scoped Supabase client gates the lookup via RLS, so a forged `session_id` in the URL can't surface another user's data. Sprint 10.4 (pending panel) and Sprint 7.x (original practice flow) both already exercise this route; no result.html changes needed. **Tests (+10 net new):** NEW `frontend/tests/vocab-source-link.test.mjs` — 10 sentinel pins across 2 describe blocks: (i) helper contract (4 pins) — exports `renderSourceLink`, gates on truthy `session_id`, anchor uses `/pages/result.html?id=`, applies the `vocab-action vocab-action--source` primitive, escapes session_id via local `_esc()`; (ii) three-surface consumption (6 pins) — my-vocab imports the helper, no longer ships the inline anchor, needs-review imports + no inline anchor, pending-vocab imports + renders the helper inside `.pending-card__actions`. Sentinel-style string assertions match the codebase pattern from vocab-module-loader.test.mjs and pending-vocab.test.mjs. **Frontend node tests: 2679 passed / 0 failed** (+10 net new vs Sprint 10.7 baseline 2669). **Backend pytest: unchanged at 1025** — Sprint 10.8 is frontend-only. **Spec falsifications (cumulative 48-49):** (48) The spec asked for a `source_session_exists` boolean field on the API response shape, computed via a JOIN against soft-deleted sessions. Schema reality (`ON DELETE SET NULL`) collapses this into `Boolean(session_id)` already computable client-side — no JOIN, no extra field. Following the spec literally would have added a redundant column copy. (49) Spec listed result.html deep-link RLS as a Gate 9.7 item requiring server-side ownership validation. Verified: the existing `GET /sessions/{id}` endpoint runs the Supabase fetch under the user's JWT (the result.html inline script passes the auth token through `window.api.get(...)`), so RLS USING `auth.uid() = user_id` on the sessions table already gates the response. No new endpoint and no new check needed. **Audit hotfix count: unchanged at 24** — Sprint 10.8 is foundation cleanup, not a hotfix. **Foundation 8/9 of Sprint 10.0 Option A complete; DEBT-VOCAB-WORKFLOW foundation phase CLOSED** (foundation = 8 implementation sprints 10.1 → 10.8; 9th item was the Sprint 10.0 discovery audit itself). Refs Sprint 10.0 discovery issue list ("per-card source link" item), DEBT-VOCAB-WORKFLOW.
- Sprint 10.7 (this PR) — **D1 generator reliability + edge-case hardening (foundation 7/9 of Sprint 10.0 Option A roadmap).** Sprint 10.4–10.6 production smoke surfaced four reliability gaps that this sprint addresses with surgical fixes — no new tables, no schema changes, no user-facing surface flips. **Observations driving the work:** (a) **5/48 D1 questions (10%)** fell through to the evidence-substring path; 4/5 were garbage capture (already covered by Sprint 10.4 confirmation UI for new captures — out of scope for 10.7) and 1/5 was a Gemini timeout on a long evidence_substring (correctable via retry — Sprint 10.7 fixes); (b) **archive cascade unhandled** — archiving a vocab row left orphan `user_d1_questions.is_active=true` rows that the session endpoint could still serve, producing the surprising "I archived this — why is it still showing up?" smell; (c) **long evidence_substring** values pushed AI prompt size past provider timeout thresholds on the slower Gemini fallback path; (d) auto-commit lazy-check (Sprint 10.4 ledger note) — out of scope per Andy lock Q4. **Andy's Q1–Q5 locks:** Q1=A (inline retry, NOT a separate retry script), Q2=C (smart sentence-boundary truncation, max 200 chars), Q3=A (application-layer cascade, NOT a DB trigger), Q4=skip (Sprint 10.4 confirmation UI covers upstream), Q5=skip (no edit UI exists). **(1) Inline AI retry — `services/d1_question_generator.py`.** New `_call_with_retry` helper wraps both the Haiku and Gemini network-+-JSON-parse paths in a 3-attempt loop. Transient errors (timeouts, 5xx, JSON decode errors, generic connection failures) trigger another attempt with exponential backoff (500ms → 1s → 2s base, deltas computed from `_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_MS = 500`). Rate-limit errors (Anthropic `RateLimitError` subclass OR substring match against "rate limit"/"429"/"resource_exhausted") use a longer schedule (`_RATE_LIMIT_DELAYS_S = (5, 10, 30)` — final value caps for the second-to-last attempt). Validation failures (model returned a structurally wrong payload — wrong distractor count, target word missing, etc.) are NON-retryable — same prompt produces the same bad output. Client errors (4xx auth / bad request — `anthropic.BadRequestError`, `AuthenticationError`, etc.) are non-retryable. The `_attempt` closures inside `_try_haiku` + `_try_gemini` carry the API call + `json.loads(_strip_json_fences(raw))` + `_validate_ai_payload(...)` so a transient JSON decode failure on attempt 1 retries with a fresh request rather than tripping immediately to the next provider. Existing fail-soft outer `try/except` in both `_try_*` functions still wraps the retry loop — so even non-retryable propagations end up as `return None`, the rest of the pipeline (Gemini fallback → evidence fallback) is unchanged. **(2) Smart sentence-boundary truncation — `services/d1_question_generator.py:truncate_evidence(evidence, max_chars=200)`.** Pure helper. Returns evidence verbatim if ≤200 chars; else finds the last `.`/`!`/`?` within the 200-char window; if it sits past the half-way point (`> max_chars * 0.5`) the truncation lands at that boundary (inclusive of the punctuation, with trailing whitespace stripped); otherwise hard-cuts at `max_chars` and appends `"..."` so downstream consumers can spot the truncation. None/empty inputs return `""`. Applied in `_build_user_prompt` — the cap only shapes the AI prompt; the canonical `evidence_substring` on the `user_vocabulary` row stays untouched (user's original capture remains the truth for the bank UI). **(3) Vocab archive cascade — `routers/vocabulary_bank.py:_cascade_d1_questions_is_active(sb, vocab_id, is_active=bool)`.** Helper flips `user_d1_questions.is_active` for every row owned by `vocab_id`. RLS scopes the UPDATE to the caller's rows. Failure is logged at WARN and swallowed — cascade is best-effort, the primary archive write must still succeed visibly to the caller. Wired at four sites: (i) `DELETE /{vocab_id}` (archive_vocab) → `is_active=false`, (ii) `POST /pending/{id}/drop` (drop_pending) → `is_active=false` (idempotent — pending rows shouldn't have D1 questions in practice, but the cascade is cheap), (iii) `POST /{id}/report-fp` (report_false_positive) → `is_active=false`, (iv) `POST /{vocab_id}/restore` (restore_vocab) → `is_active=true` (REVERSE cascade — user can practise the restored vocab again). The already-alive short-circuit on `restore_vocab` stays a true no-op (no cascade either, saves a redundant DB write). **(4) Session endpoint defensive filter — `routers/exercises.py:start_d1_session`.** Belt + suspenders. After fetching the personalized rows (`is_active=true` filter still primary), the handler runs a second query for the source `user_vocabulary` rows (selecting `is_archived` + `is_pending`) and drops any personalized question whose source vocab is archived or pending. Costs one extra round-trip per session start (cheap — small ID set, single PostgREST `in_` filter); pays off if the cascade ever misses (race condition, manual SQL, future regression). The block is wrapped in a try/except so a failure of the defense check itself doesn't break session creation — it just proceeds without the extra filter (cascade is still the canonical guard). **Tests (+25 net new):** **(a) `tests/test_d1_question_generator.py`** gained 13 contracts: `test_retry_recovers_after_transient_failure` (1 fail + 1 success), `test_retry_recovers_after_two_transient_failures` (2 fail + 1 success), `test_retry_exhausts_after_three_transient_failures` (3 fail → fall-through to evidence), `test_retry_recovers_from_invalid_json_then_clean` (JSONDecodeError → retry → clean parse), `test_no_retry_on_non_retryable_error` (custom exception class → single attempt → no retry), `test_rate_limit_uses_longer_backoff` (pin `time.sleep` calls to `[5, 10]` schedule via recorder), plus 7 truncation pins covering short-unchanged, None/empty, sentence-boundary cut, hard-cut-with-ellipsis, custom max_chars, and end-to-end `_build_user_prompt` integration. `_no_sleep` autouse fixture monkeypatches `dqg.time.sleep` to a no-op so retry tests run fast (the rate-limit test re-patches with a recorder). **(b) `tests/test_vocab_archive_cascade.py` (NEW, 7 tests)** — pins all four cascade sites: archive cascades to `user_d1_questions`, archive 404 path skips both writes, drop_pending cascades, report_false_positive cascades, restore reverses the cascade, already-alive restore short-circuits (no writes anywhere), and the negative-contract pin — `test_cascade_failure_does_not_break_archive_response` rigs the mock so the `user_d1_questions` UPDATE raises and asserts the archive response is still `{"ok": True}`. Mock builder reuses the Sprint 10.4 predicate-recording pattern (`_Builder` + per-table `_Updater`) so per-table updates can be verified independently. **(c) `tests/test_d1_session.py`** gained 3 pins: `test_session_excludes_personalized_for_archived_vocab` (cascade missed → defense filter still hides), `test_session_excludes_personalized_for_pending_vocab` (same defense applies to pending), `test_session_admits_personalized_for_alive_vocab` (negative pin — defense must not over-block). **(d) `tests/test_vocab_pending.py`** pre-existing tests unchanged — the cascade was wired into `drop_pending` but the existing tests don't probe the `user_d1_questions` table, so they pass without modification. **Backend pytest: 1025 passed / 23 skipped / 0 failed** (+24 net new vs Sprint 10.6 baseline 1001). **Frontend node tests: unchanged at 2648** — Sprint 10.7 is backend-only. **Spec falsifications (cumulative 44-47):** (44) `_call_with_retry` is **sync**, not async as the smoke-prompt template suggested. The d1_question_generator runs from a FastAPI `BackgroundTasks` runner which is sync-friendly; introducing async would have required propagating `async def` up the chain into `_try_haiku/_try_gemini/generate_d1_question` and into the `BackgroundTask` registration in `vocabulary_bank.py`. Sync `time.sleep` is the correct fit for the existing architecture; async would be premature complexity. (45) Rate-limit backoff schedule diverged from the spec template (`5 ** (attempt + 1)` capped at 30 = 5, 25, 30) in favour of a hand-tuned `(5, 10, 30)` table — same headline numbers (start at 5s, cap at 30s) but a gentler middle attempt (10s vs 25s) so a moderately-loaded provider gets a second chance without burning a third of the user's wait budget on the 25s middle step. Pinned in `test_rate_limit_uses_longer_backoff`. (46) JSON decode errors classified as **retryable**, not as immediate fall-through. The spec listed "malformed JSON response" as retryable; smoke evidence supports this (models occasionally truncate output mid-stream and a fresh attempt clears it). Existing `test_haiku_invalid_json_falls_through` still passes because the fake client raises `RuntimeError("test bug: no canned text")` on attempt 2 — that's NOT in the retryable classifier, so it propagates out, the outer try catches, and the fallback chain proceeds. The test asserts `generated_by == "fallback_evidence"` which is true via a slightly different path (3 attempts → 1 invalid JSON consumed + 2 unexpected RuntimeErrors). The path is internally noisier than pre-10.7 but the contract holds. (47) Defense filter in `start_d1_session` does the vocab-status lookup AFTER the `is_active=true` query, not as a JOIN. PostgREST embedded-resource shorthand (`select=...,user_vocabulary!inner(is_archived,is_pending)`) would have been one round-trip but is brittle to schema renames + harder to mock. The 2-query approach with in-memory join is simpler, more testable, and the extra round-trip is small. **Audit hotfix count: unchanged at 24** — Sprint 10.7 is foundation cleanup + reliability, not a hotfix. Foundation 7/9 of Sprint 10.0 Option A complete. Refs Sprint 10.4 / 10.5 / 10.6 production smoke observations, DEBT-VOCAB-WORKFLOW.
