- Sprint 7.13.1-hotfix (PR #183) — **RED chrome regression: user pill stuck on placeholder across all 5 grammar pages post Sprint 7.13.** Andy reported grammar.html user pill never populates with display name + avatar initials — stays at the HTML default `…` / `·` indefinitely. Andy's per-page audit (`grep -c "initSupabase"` across all 18 migrated chrome pages) surfaced the omission: **5 grammar pages ship `<script src="…supabase-js@2">` + `<script src="…/api.js">` BUT never call `initSupabase(SUPABASE_URL, SUPABASE_ANON)`** — the canonical bootstrap that exposes `window.getSupabase` on the global. Confirmed pages: `frontend/grammar.html`, `frontend/pages/grammar-roadmap.html`, `frontend/pages/grammar-article.html`, `frontend/pages/grammar-search.html`, `frontend/pages/grammar-compare.html`. The 13 other migrated chrome pages all have the full init pattern (12 in `frontend/pages/` + `frontend/onboarding.html` at root). **Root cause:** the Sprint 7.11-built `<aver-chrome>` component polls `window.getSupabase` every 50ms × 60 tries (~3s ceiling) on `connectedCallback`. When `initSupabase()` never runs, `window.getSupabase` stays undefined; the poll exhausts its tries and logs `[aver-chrome] window.getSupabase unavailable after polling; pill placeholder retained.` — pill defaults persist. The bug is **pre-existing on the grammar cluster** since Sprint 6.15 (when the editorial pages first received chrome) — but it was masked because the legacy chrome's `/js/user-pill.js` `populateUserPill()` ran the same getSupabase check defensively and **silently no-op'd if Supabase wasn't initialized** (early-return at `if (!sb || !sb.auth || typeof sb.auth.getSession !== 'function') return;`). The pill placeholder stayed visible in production for an unknown duration without surfacing the underlying config gap. Sprint 7.12/7.13 chrome migration surfaced the latent bug only because the component logs a warning on poll exhaustion (where the legacy module did not) — making the missing-init state observable. **Atomic 5-page fix:** Python script regex-matched each grammar page's `<script src="…/api.js"></script>` line + injected the canonical init block immediately after (copied verbatim from `frontend/pages/home.html` lines 147-152, including the exact SUPABASE_URL `https://nqhrtqspznepmveyurzm.supabase.co` + SUPABASE_ANON `sb_publishable_a_vDrA0c3mT-QlASPW7yhw_YZnUsfT4`). The injected block carries a Sprint 7.13.1-hotfix marker comment explaining the contract (`<aver-chrome>`'s `window.getSupabase` poll resolves once init runs). Every page reported `api.js match count = 1` confirming clean replacement. **NEW sentinel pin** in `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` (~20 pins added under describe block "Sprint 7.13.1-hotfix — every `<aver-chrome>` page must call initSupabase()"): per-page assertion `\binitSupabase\s*\(` regex on all 18 `MIGRATED_PAGES` entries + 1 canonical-URL sentinel asserting `https://nqhrtqspznepmveyurzm.supabase.co` appears in each migrated page (catches a page being pointed at a different Supabase project, a different drift class). Sentinel locks the post-fix state so any future migrated page that ships supabase-js + api.js without `initSupabase()` fails CI. **Gate 11 candidacy formalized in this hotfix:** Codex visual audits + Sprint 6.17 → 6.20 chrome contract sweeps verified markup parity (`.topnav-wrap` + `.brand` + `.user-pill` IDs present) and CSS rule integrity (foundation tokens + canonical chrome rules in `components.css`). **None verified that the page's `<script>` initialization order actually exposes `window.getSupabase` before the component mounts.** The same class of gap also explains why Sprint 7.7-hotfix (vocab modules unstyled — missing Tailwind import on parent) + this hotfix slipped: markup contract ≠ runtime resource contract. **Gate 11 — "Embedded-host resource parity + chrome contract verification":** every page hosting a chrome-dependent component must (a) load the canonical script-set in the canonical order; (b) call the canonical init bootstrap; (c) expose the global the component contracts against. Filed informally in Sprint 7.7-hotfix + Sprint 7.8-hotfix; promoted to formal gate candidacy in this hotfix. **Sprint 7.14 will formalize Gate 11** in `DESIGN_SYSTEM.md § 17`. **Test result:** 182/182 in `chrome-unification-canonical` (+19 net Sprint 7.13.1 pins). Full frontend gate: 2540/2545 pass — same 5 pre-existing failures from Sprint 7.13 baseline (chrome-spacing 6.18 Cat A flashcards/exercises wrapper padding + subheading 6.19 flashcards/exercises eyebrow + 6.16.1 stale audit count assertion) — all scoped to Sprint 7.14 cleanup per the original Sprint 7.13 prompt anti-pattern. **Audit hotfix count 16 → 17** (Sprint 7.13.1-hotfix IS audit hotfix — RED chrome regression that escaped Sprint 7.12 + 7.13 phased migration's smoke). **Honest retrospection:** the missing-init gap pre-existed on grammar pages since Sprint 6.15 chrome adoption — Sprint 7.12 + 7.13 phased migration's smoke (per the prompts' Phase D checklists) called for "user pill populates with Supabase user data (after login)" verification but evidently the manual checks didn't catch grammar pages specifically. The component's defensive polling masked the failure mode as "pill stays placeholder" rather than a hard error, which is the kindest possible failure but also the most silent. Gate 11 candidacy + the new initSupabase sentinel close this class of bug at the markup-audit layer: any future migrated page that ships supabase-js + api.js without `initSupabase()` will fail CI immediately, no manual smoke required. **Pre-push verification:** `grep -rn "SUPABASE_URL\|SUPABASE_ANON" .github/` → no matches (no CI references to lift). **Sprint 7.14 scope updated to include:** retiring `components.css` chrome rules (original scope) + Gate 11 formalization (Sprint 7.13.1-hotfix candidacy promotion) + fixing 5 pre-existing test pin staleness issues (flashcards/exercises wrapper padding + eyebrow pins post Sprint 7.4/7.5 vocab module migration + 6.16.1 audit count assertion bumped to current 17).

- Sprint 7.11 (PR #180) — **Build sprint — `<aver-chrome>` Web Component shipped (additive only; ZERO page migrations).** Phase 2/5 of the chrome unification refactor authorized by Sprint 7.10 approval. Pattern mirrors Sprint 7.3 my-vocab module build (the first DEBT-09-B implementation sprint that delivered ~4h actual on budget). Sprint 7.11 ships the additive component module + source-pin contract + smoke fixture; Sprint 7.12+ migrates pages to consume it. **Phase A audit (JSDOM dependency strategy)** surfaced a clean decision: the repo carries **no `package.json`, no `node_modules`, no transpile step**; CI runs `node --test` directly with the explicit inline-doc principle "*The frontend tests are pure node:test files — no transpile, no bundler. They exercise contracts (HTML structure, CSS token discipline, theme-toggle exports, IIFE patterns) rather than rendered behavior, so a single Node setup with no dependencies is enough.*" Adding JSDOM as a devDep would require creating `package.json` from scratch, an `npm install` CI step, ~5MB of vendored code (alternative), and breaking the "no dependencies" contract for the marginal benefit of render-fixture testing. **Decision: source-pin-only fallback** documented in the Sprint 7.11 prompt as Phase A audit outcome. Trade-off: rendering verification deferred to Sprint 7.12 page-migration smoke (per-page mounted in real browser) + smoke fixture HTML for ad-hoc browser checks. Coverage floor: ~30 source-pin sentinels in `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` cover structural contract + API surface + lifecycle callbacks + token usage. **Atomic deliverables:** (1) **NEW** `frontend/js/components/aver-chrome.js` (~580 LOC, ES module) — `AverChrome` class extends `HTMLElement`, `static get observedAttributes() { return ['active']; }`, attaches shadow root (`mode: 'open'`) on `connectedCallback`, renders the canonical chrome template byte-equivalent to `components.css` lines 741-923 + lines 116-130 inline as `<style>`, idempotent mount via `_mounted` flag, public `setUser({ name?, initials?, email? })` method that writes pill + avatar via canonical 2-letter initials and marks `_userOverride = true` so the auto-fetch path skips. Public `av-chrome-signed-out` `CustomEvent` (`bubbles: true, composed: true`) dispatched right before the `/index.html` redirect. **Imports for reuse:** `bindToggleButton` from `/js/theme-toggle.js` (works on shadow-tree button — `addEventListener` doesn't care about the shadow boundary; teardown function returned for cleanup) + `canonicalInitials` from `/js/user-pill.js` (single source of truth for the 2-letter algorithm; not re-implemented). **Theme-aware icon swap:** `:host-context([data-theme="dark"]) .av-theme-toggle .icon-sun { display: block }` substitutes for the page-level `[data-theme="dark"] .av-theme-toggle .icon-sun` rule — `:host-context()` looks up the tree past the shadow host to find ancestor matches, so the page-level `<html data-theme>` keeps driving the icon swap inside the shadow root (W3C CSS Shadow Parts spec, all major browsers per January 2026 cutoff). **Supabase polling pattern (Phase B Q5):** `POLL_INTERVAL_MS = 50` × `POLL_MAX_TRIES = 60` = ~3s ceiling; recursive `setTimeout(tick, 50)` until `window.getSupabase` is available, then `sb.auth.getSession()` → write pill + avatar if still on placeholder values (`'…'` / `'·'`) and `_userOverride` is false. Silently times out + logs warning if Supabase never appears. **AbortController for cleanup:** dropdown + logout listeners attached with `{ signal }` so `disconnectedCallback()` abort-cancels everything in one call; doc-level click + keydown listeners tracked separately via `_docClickHandler` / `_docKeydownHandler` for explicit removal; poll timer cleared via `clearTimeout(this._pollTimer)`. **Outside-click via `composedPath()`:** the dropdown closes when the click does NOT pass through this host element, using `e.composedPath().includes(this)` — composed events bubble through shadow boundaries so the host comparison is the correct check, not `toggle.parentElement.contains(e.target)` (which is the open DOM idiom that breaks across shadow roots). (2) **NEW** `frontend/tests/fixtures/aver-chrome-smoke.html` — standalone smoke page mountable via `cd frontend && python3 -m http.server 8080`; renders the component with anti-flash IIFE in `<head>` + tokens/base/components CSS + dev controls (active-attribute buttons, setUser buttons, av-chrome-signed-out event log). Smoke does NOT include Supabase init — pill remains on placeholder unless `setUser()` runs. (3) **EXTENDED** `frontend/tests/chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` — 2 new `describe` blocks (~30 source-pin tests): **"Sprint 7.11 — `<aver-chrome>` Web Component contract"** pins class declaration + `observedAttributes ['active']` + `customElements.define` registration + 2 module imports (`bindToggleButton` / `canonicalInitials`) + Shadow DOM `mode: 'open'` attach + `setUser` method signature + `_userOverride` flag + `connectedCallback` orchestration sequence (shadow attach → render → applyActive → bindToggle → bindDropdown → bindLogout → schedulePopulate) + `attributeChangedCallback` filters on `'active'` + `disconnectedCallback` cleans up all 5 owned resources + `av-chrome-signed-out` CustomEvent with `composed: true` + `signOut()` in try/catch + `POLL_INTERVAL_MS` / `POLL_MAX_TRIES` constants + `AbortController` usage + `VALID_ACTIVE` enum exactly 5 skills + brand wordmark with `<span class="dot">` + 5 `data-tab` attrs + 2 `.locked` spans (Reading + Listening) + theme toggle SVG icons + user pill + dropdown + 2 menu items + ARIA preservation + `--av-*` token usage in inline style + `:host-context([data-theme="dark"])` for icon swap + `:host { display: block }` + no `window.*` handler leaks + idempotent `_mounted` guard + canonical hrefs on all 5 skill links. **"Sprint 7.11 — additive build only, NO page migrations"** pins zero `<aver-chrome>` references in any of the 18 canonical chrome pages (Sprint 7.12+ scope guard) + `components.css` chrome rules still present (Sprint 7.14 will retire) + `user-pill.js` / `theme-toggle.js` keep their `DOMContentLoaded` auto-bind branches through Sprint 7.11 (Sprint 7.12 refactors them to remove top-level auto-bind so the component owns init). **Tests:** 218/218 in `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` pass (+33 net: 30 new Sprint 7.11 contract pins + 3 new "no-migration" guards). **Frontend gate:** unchanged baseline + 33 new pins. CI allowlist not modified — the extended `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` runs in the same `frontend` job as before (no new test file needed because all pins live in the existing canonical suite). **Audit hotfix count unchanged at 16** (Sprint 7.11 is additive build, not gate work or hotfix). **NO scope creep confirmed:** zero page migrations (all 18 chrome pages byte-identical) — Sprint 7.12 batch 1 (home / speaking / writing-dashboard / vocabulary / grammar) follows; zero `components.css` chrome-rule deletion (Sprint 7.14 scope); zero `user-pill.js` / `theme-toggle.js` refactor (Sprint 7.12 scope); zero slots (Phase B Q3); zero light DOM variant (Phase B Q1); zero footer/sidebar/eyebrow primitives (Phase B Q7). **Architectural moment:** the chrome contract is now provably encapsulated in a single self-contained module. Sprint 7.12 page migrations become **mechanical** — replace the ~40-line chrome block + supporting script tags with `<aver-chrome active="...">` + one `<script type="module" src="/js/components/aver-chrome.js"></script>` — no per-page binding logic, no per-page Lucide hydration MutationObserver, no per-page user-pill populate inline script. The component owns all of it. **Effort:** 3-4h estimated, ~3h actual (faster than estimate because source-pin path avoided JSDOM dependency engineering). **Pre-push verification:** `grep -rn "aver-chrome" .github/` → no stale CI refs (existing chrome-unification suite already runs in the `frontend` job, no new allowlist entry required); `package.json` absent at repo root + frontend root (vanilla static HTML project confirmed).
- Sprint 7.10 (PR #179) — **Approval + prompt sprint — Andy locks Sprint 7.9 Phase B answers and authorizes the Sprint 7.11 build. Pure docs sprint; zero production code modified, zero tests modified.** Follows the discovery→approval→implementation pattern established by Sprint 7.1→7.2→7.3 (which delivered DEBT-2026-05-09-B on the original 22h estimate with 0 hotfixes). Andy's 7 Phase B answers locked: **(Q1) Shadow DOM** — chosen as the platform-level guarantee against CSS override drift (the recurring bug class behind 6.10.1 / 6.15.4-7 hotfixes / 7.8-hotfix vocabulary.css `.brand` override); Shadow DOM closes the class at the boundary because page rules cannot leak into the chrome and chrome rules cannot leak out, while CSS custom properties (`--av-*` tokens) cross the boundary natively per W3C CSS Custom Properties Module Level 1. **(Q2) `active` attribute** — single attribute on the custom element with enum `home` / `writing` / `speaking` / `grammar` / `vocabulary`; "none" is implicit when unset (no `active="none"` ceremony). Reactive via `observedAttributes = ['active']` + `attributeChangedCallback(name, prev, next)` so future page-level state changes can flip the highlighted tab without re-rendering. **(Q3) Slots-free** — no `<slot>` escape hatches on the canonical 18 pages; the contract is "render the canonical chrome exactly, no overrides." Keeps migration mechanical (no per-page slot wiring), and if a legitimate override case surfaces later it can be added in a future minor without breaking the existing API. **(Q4) `setUser(data)` method** — preserves the speaking.html `renderUser` permissions-context override pattern from Sprint 7.8-hotfix through a typed API instead of DOM-poking across the Shadow DOM boundary; placeholder-detection contract (`textContent === '…'` / `'·'`) inverts to "explicit override always wins" inside the component (page-authoritative source defers via method call, not DOM mutation). **(Q5) Polling `window.getSupabase`** — defensive against Supabase init race; matches the existing bootstrap pattern in user-pill.js Sprint 7.8-hotfix (DOMContentLoaded → wait for getSupabase availability → invoke). Avoids hard-failing if the component mounts before the inline Supabase init script runs. **(Q6) Batched migration** — Sprint 7.11 build only (no page migrations) → Sprint 7.12 batch 1 (5 skill landing pages: home / speaking / writing-dashboard / vocabulary / grammar) → Sprint 7.13 batch 2 (13 sub-pages: practice / result / full-test-result / writing-result / my-vocabulary / flashcards / exercises / profile / onboarding / grammar-roadmap / grammar-search / grammar-compare / grammar-article) → Sprint 7.14 cleanup (delete `components.css` chrome block + redundant rules in `home.css` / `vocabulary.css` / `grammar-wiki.css` + retire stale test pins + file Gate 11 candidacy). Total estimated effort ~10-13h across 4 PRs, matching the Sprint 7.1→7.6 phased migration calibration. **(Q7) Explicit out-of-scope:** footer + sidebar (separate non-blocking refactor; chrome ≠ full layout); `.eyebrow` primitive (page-level concern, Sprint 6.19 already shipped); admin pages (out of scope — admin pages have their own chrome family per Phase 4 Cat 5); marketing pages `index.html` / `pricing.html` (out of scope — Cat 4 marketing tier); anti-flash theme IIFE stays in `<head>` per page (must run before any stylesheet to prevent FOUC; the component handles `<style>` inline but cannot own the anti-flash script because the IIFE must execute pre-paint). **Sprint 7.11 build prompt committed** at `docs/sprint-7-11-prompt-aver-chrome-build.md` (~485 lines, 10 sections): scope (in/out), Phase B approvals table, component contract (file layout `frontend/js/components/aver-chrome.js` + `frontend/tests/aver-chrome.test.js`; public API surface `AverChrome` class extends `HTMLElement` + `observedAttributes = ['active']` + `setUser(data)` method + `av-chrome-signed-out` custom event; shadow tree structure mirroring canonical chrome byte-for-byte; inline `<style>` block sourced from `components.css` lines 741-923; lifecycle callbacks `connectedCallback` shadow attach + render + apply active + bind toggle + bind dropdown + bind logout + schedule populate / `attributeChangedCallback` for reactive active highlighting / `disconnectedCallback` AbortController-driven teardown), test strategy (extend `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` with source-pin layer + NEW JSDOM render fixture `aver-chrome.test.js`), phase breakdown (Phase A 30 min audit JSDOM dependency strategy — vendor vs npm-install vs source-pin-only; Phase B 1.5-2h code synthesis; Phase C 1-1.5h tests; Phase D 30 min smoke; total 3-4h), acceptance criteria checklist, NO scope creep list (no page migrations, no `components.css` deletion, no `user-pill.js` refactor, no `theme-toggle.js` refactor, no slots, no light DOM, no footer/sidebar/eyebrow), pre-push verification command (`grep -rn "aver-chrome" .github/ package.json`), PR title template (`feat(chrome): build <aver-chrome> Web Component (Sprint 7.11 — phase 2/5)`), after-merge plan. **Frontend gate:** unchanged from Sprint 7.9 baseline (no test modifications). **Audit hotfix count unchanged at 16** (Sprint 7.10 is approval + docs, not gate work or hotfix). **Open question deferred to Sprint 7.11 Phase A** (not pre-decided): JSDOM dependency strategy — `package.json` carries no `jsdom` dev-dep today, so Phase A audits the three options (vendor JSDOM into `frontend/tests/_vendor/`, npm-install `jsdom` as devDependency, fallback to source-pin-only coverage if neither lands cleanly) before writing the `aver-chrome.test.js` render fixture; source-pin coverage in `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` is the floor, render fixture is the ceiling. **Architectural framing:** Sprint 7.10 is the **approval gate**, not the build gate. Locking the 7 Phase B answers in this ledger row gives Sprint 7.11 a contractual reference — if Sprint 7.11 deviates from any Q1-Q7 decision, this ledger entry is the audit anchor against which the deviation is reviewed.
- Sprint 7.9 (PR #178) — **Discovery sprint — chrome Web Component architecture audit. Sprint 7.9 = audit + design proposal. **Phase A inventory:** 18 pages audited (home / speaking / practice / result / full-test-result / writing-dashboard / writing-result / vocabulary / my-vocabulary / flashcards / exercises / profile / onboarding / grammar / grammar-roadmap / grammar-search / grammar-compare / grammar-article). All ship the canonical `.topnav-wrap` + `.topnav` markup byte-identical post Sprint 6.17 → 6.20 chrome unification — only the `class="active"` placement varies per page. Three CSS files contain chrome rules outside `components.css`: `home.css` (redundant canonical duplicates), `vocabulary.css` (redundant duplicates; 1.35rem `.brand` override already removed Sprint 7.8-hotfix), `grammar-wiki.css` (font-family scoping fix from Sprint 7.8-hotfix — required because the page body switches to DM Sans for editorial typography § 14.2, and the override blocks the body cascade from reaching chrome). **Phase A also documented:** the canonical script-set pattern (Supabase CDN → api.js → initSupabase inline → theme-toggle.js binding → user-pill.js auto-load + Lucide hydration MutationObserver); the user-pill async flow (DOMContentLoaded → bindUserPill + populateUserPill → Supabase getSession → write `#user-pill-name` + `#user-avatar` with placeholder-detection); the eyebrow + secondary-nav scope (page-content level, NEVER inside chrome). **Web Component API designed:** `<aver-chrome>` custom element, **Shadow DOM** (closes the per-page CSS override drift class at the platform level — page rules cannot leak in, chrome rules cannot leak out, CSS custom properties `--av-*` cross the boundary natively), single `active` attribute (enum: `home` / `writing` / `speaking` / `grammar` / `vocabulary`), **slots-free** (no escape hatches for the canonical 18 pages — keeps migration mechanical), **auto-fetch user state** via `window.getSupabase()` matching the existing `populateUserPill` contract from Sprint 7.8-hotfix, **inline `<style>` in shadow root** (FOUC prevention, ~150 LOC self-contained), `setUser(...)` method on the custom element for the speaking.html `renderUser` permissions-context pattern (preserves the Sprint 7.8-hotfix placeholder-detection contract through a typed API instead of DOM-poking across the shadow boundary). **Phased migration outlined:** Sprint 7.10 Andy approval (30 min) → 7.11 build component (3-4h, additive — no migration yet) → 7.12 batch 1 skill landings (5 pages, ~2h) → 7.13 batch 2 sub-pages (13 pages, ~2h) → 7.14 cleanup (delete redundant chrome rules from `home.css` / `vocabulary.css` / `grammar-wiki.css`, delete `components.css` chrome block, retire test pins, file Gate 11 candidacy). **Total estimate ~10-13h** (matches Sprint 7.1 → 7.6 methodology calibration). **Risks documented:** anti-flash IIFE ordering preserved (CSS custom properties cross shadow boundary per spec); Supabase init race (recommend polling pattern); speaking.html renderUser cross-shadow override (recommend `setUser` method); grammar-wiki.css font-family override becomes unnecessary post-migration (Shadow DOM auto-isolates); Vercel rewrite paths require absolute hrefs (Sprint 6.15.8-hotfix lesson); ES module side-effect cleanup (refactor user-pill.js / theme-toggle.js to remove top-level auto-bind so the Web Component owns init); test strategy = source-pin (~80% coverage) + JSDOM render fixture (full coverage). **Recommendation document committed at** `docs/sprint-7-9-chrome-web-component-discovery.md` (~600 lines: problem statement + 18-page inventory + API design + per-page migration diff + risks + effort estimate + Phase B questions for Andy). **Frontend gate:** unchanged from Sprint 7.8-hotfix baseline (no test modifications). **Audit hotfix count unchanged at 16** (Sprint 7.9 is discovery, not gate work). **Predicted long-term impact** (Sprint 7.10 → 7.14 closure): ~720 LOC chrome markup deleted across 18 pages + ~80 LOC redundant CSS removed + ~40 LOC per-page inline scripts retired + ~150 LOC components.css chrome block deletable = ~−850 LOC; ~+250 LOC for the new component module + ~+80 LOC for JSDOM test fixture = **net ~−600 LOC**. Drift class extinguished at the markup layer: future "Sprint X.x-hotfix: chrome inconsistency on page Y" cannot recur because there is no markup duplication to drift.
- Sprint 7.8-hotfix (PR #177) — **RED chrome consistency regression: 3 distinct bugs flagged from Andy's visual review post Sprint 7.7-hotfix merge.** Codex 9/9 GREEN baseline from Sprint 6.17.x → 6.20 was broken by drift that accumulated across the Sprint 7.x module migration cluster. **Bug 1 — logo size drift (3 sizes across 5 pages).** Phase A grep traced two confirmed CSS root causes: (a) `frontend/css/vocabulary.css` lines 66-74 contained an explicit `.brand { font-size: 1.35rem; ... }` override redeclaring the canonical rule with a hardcoded larger font-size and literal font-family (`'Plus Jakarta Sans', ui-sans-serif, system-ui, sans-serif` vs canonical `var(--av-font-sans)` token); pre-existing Sprint 6.10 drift that escaped chrome-unification work and surfaced visually only after Sprint 7.7-hotfix added Tailwind CDN + module CSS to vocabulary.html (the additional imports changed the rendered context enough to make the size difference obvious); (b) `frontend/css/grammar-wiki.css` line 38-51 sets `body.av-page { font-family: 'DM Sans', ui-sans-serif, system-ui }` per § 14.2 editorial sub-system decision — DM Sans was intended for article body content but cascaded into `.brand` because the chrome inherits font-family from `body`. DM Sans renders at visually-different glyph proportions vs Plus Jakarta Sans at the same `1.125rem`, making the chrome look "smaller" on grammar pages. **Bug 2 — user pill stuck on "..."  on writing-dashboard / grammar / vocabulary.** Root cause: `frontend/js/user-pill.js` originally only bound the dropdown toggle + sign-out — it never populated `#user-pill-name` or `#user-avatar`. Population was per-page inline JS shipped on home.html (lines 220-242) and speaking.html (`renderUser` lines 1017-1031), but the 3 broken pages had **no populate logic** so the HTML defaults `…` and `·` stayed forever. **Bug 3 — initials inconsistency.** Same user "Vinh Tran" rendered as "V" on home.html (line 233: `(name[0] || '·').toUpperCase()` — 1-letter) vs "VT" on speaking.html (line 1029: `name.split(' ').map(w => w[0]).join('').slice(0, 2).toUpperCase()` — 2-letter). Two algorithms in production, single source of truth violation. **Phase B canonical decision: 2 letters.** Matches the Sprint 6.17.1 speaking.html implementation, naturally handles single-name case via `slice(0, 2)` (e.g., `"Vinh".split(' ').map(w => w[0])` → `["V"]` → "V"). Supersedes the 1-letter home.html legacy. **Atomic fixes:** (1) **MODIFIED** `frontend/css/vocabulary.css` — deleted the `.brand` rule + `.brand .dot` rule (lines 66-74), replaced with an explanatory comment. Canonical components.css `.brand` (font-size `var(--av-fs-lg)` = 1.125rem, font-family `var(--av-font-sans)` = Plus Jakarta Sans) now wins. (2) **MODIFIED** `frontend/css/grammar-wiki.css` — added explicit `body.av-page .topnav-wrap, body.av-page .topnav, body.av-page .brand, body.av-page .nav-links, body.av-page .topnav-right { font-family: var(--av-font-sans); }` rule after the `body.av-page` DM Sans declaration. Chrome keeps Plus Jakarta Sans even on editorial pages; article body (`.article-body`, headings via Lora) preserves the § 14.2 sub-system. (3) **MODIFIED** `frontend/js/user-pill.js` — extended from dropdown-only binding to dropdown + populate. NEW exports `canonicalInitials(name)` (canonical 2-letter algorithm — single function = single source of truth) and `async populateUserPill()` (reads Supabase session, writes `#user-pill-name` truncated >14 chars + `#user-avatar` via `canonicalInitials`). Idempotent via `data-user-pill-populated` flag; placeholder-detection skips overwrite if a page-specific bootstrap (e.g., speaking.html `renderUser` with permissions context) has already populated the pill — defers to the page-authoritative source. DOMContentLoaded handler runs both `bindUserPill()` + `populateUserPill()`. (4) **MODIFIED** `frontend/pages/home.html` — deleted the duplicated 1-letter inline bootstrap (lines 220-242), keeping only the auth-gate redirect. user-pill.js now owns population canonically. Speaking.html `renderUser` left alone — it correctly produces 2-letter initials matching the new canonical algorithm AND is part of a larger `/auth/me` fetch with permissions context; placeholder-detection in `populateUserPill` defers to it on speaking. **Tests:** (a) **EXTENDED** `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` Sprint 6.17 foundation suite — 5 new pins under `/js/user-pill.js`: exports `populateUserPill` + `canonicalInitials`; canonical 2-letter algorithm signature (`.split(/\s+/)` + `.slice(0, 2)` + `.toUpperCase()`); placeholder-detection (`textContent === '…'` + `'·'`); idempotency guard (`data-user-pill-populated`); auto-bind runs both `bindUserPill()` + `populateUserPill()`. (b) **NEW** describe block "Sprint 7.8-hotfix — `.brand` chrome consistency across pages" — 3 pins: vocabulary.css must NOT redeclare `.brand` (regression guard against the 1.35rem override returning); grammar-wiki.css must keep `.brand` on `var(--av-font-sans)` explicitly (regression guard against DM Sans cascading into chrome again); components.css canonical `.brand` rule uses `var(--av-fs-lg)` + `var(--av-font-sans)` tokens (the source-of-truth pin). **Frontend gate: 186/186 pass in chrome-unification-canonical** + full CI allowlist green. **Audit hotfix count 15 → 16** (Sprint 7.8-hotfix IS audit hotfix — RED visual + functional regression that escaped Sprint 7.7-hotfix's smoke). **Honest retrospection note:** Codex 9/9 GREEN baseline from Sprint 6.17.x → 6.20 was a markup-contract verification — the audit checked that the canonical `.brand`, `.user-pill`, etc. markup existed across pages, but did NOT verify (a) that no per-page CSS overrode the canonical rules (vocabulary.css `.brand` slipped) or (b) that chrome JS contracts had populate parity (user-pill.js missing populate, requiring per-page inline bootstraps that drifted to 1-letter vs 2-letter initials). Sprint 7.x migrations exposed both because Tailwind CDN addition (7.7-hotfix) made the size delta legible and module mounts made the missing populate scripts more visible. Same Gate 11 candidacy filed informally in Sprint 7.7-hotfix applies here: an "embedded-host resource parity + chrome contract verification" gate would have caught both — chrome contract is more than markup, it's the JS+CSS execution that produces a consistent rendered surface. Not formalized this sprint to keep hotfix surgical.
- Sprint 7.7-hotfix (PR #176) — **RED visual regression hotfix: vocab modules unstyled when embedded into vocabulary.html.** Andy reported (post Sprint 7.6 merge) that all 3 vocab tabs (my-vocab / flashcards / exercises) render unstyled when accessed via the unified `/pages/vocabulary.html` landing — buttons in default browser style, all 4 UI states (loading / error / empty / data) stacking simultaneously because `.hidden` Tailwind utility doesn't resolve. **Phase A root cause:** Sprint 7.3 → 7.6 migrations moved each child's page body into JS module template literals BUT did not migrate the resource imports — each standalone shell (`my-vocabulary.html`, `flashcards.html`, `exercises.html`) loads `<script src="https://cdn.tailwindcss.com">` + custom Tailwind config + `/css/<module>.css` + `/css/ds.css` in its own `<head>`; the parent `vocabulary.html` had **none of those imports**, so when modules mount embedded their templates rely on classes that don't resolve. Confirmed via `grep "rel=\"stylesheet\"" vocabulary.html` (only foundation + `vocabulary.css`) vs the 3 standalone shells (each carrying Tailwind + per-module CSS + `ds.css`). Standalone path unaffected — bug is parent-side only. **Why this slipped Sprint 7.3 / 7.4 / 7.5 Phase D smoke:** smoke checks pinned "tab switches smooth" + "module mounts" — they fired the mount + saw the template HTML appear in DOM. Without visual diff vs the standalone shell, the unstyled render read as "it works, looks roughly right." Classic Gate 10 (Sprint 6.20) blind-spot pattern — *markup correct ≠ resource-loaded-correct*. **Phase B option analysis:** **Option A — eager load** (chosen). Add 5 imports to vocabulary.html `<head>`: Tailwind CDN script + canonical Tailwind config (navy/teal + Plus Jakarta Sans, matching standalone shells) + 3 per-module CSS links (`my-vocabulary.css` + `flashcards.css` + `exercises.css`). Simplest fix, smallest blast radius, no module API changes; ~35 KB total additional CSS, cached after any standalone visit. **Option B — lazy inject via `_loader.js`** (rejected): more "module-pattern pure" but requires modifying 3 modules + helper + tests for a hotfix; surface area not warranted for RED visual regression fix. **Option C — inline CSS string in module** (rejected): heaviest refactor, out of hotfix scope. **`ds.css` skipped** — grep confirmed zero `.ds-*` references in any of the 3 modules or their CSS files; the standalone shells link it as historical/cosmetic dead weight. **Atomic fix:** `frontend/pages/vocabulary.html` `<head>` gains 5 imports + explanatory Sprint 7.7-hotfix comment block explaining the contract (modules render embedded ⇒ parent must supply Tailwind + per-module CSS). **Test:** new pin in `vocab-module-loader.test.mjs` section 4 — "Sprint 7.7-hotfix — vocab module resources eagerly loaded for embedded path" — verifies Tailwind CDN `<script>` present, Tailwind config has Plus Jakarta Sans (Sprint 6.10 typography contract), and all 3 module CSS files linked. Drop of any one import fails the test. **Frontend gate: 73/73 in vocab-module-loader pass + full CI allowlist green.** **Audit hotfix count 14 → 15** (Sprint 7.7-hotfix IS audit hotfix — RED visual regression that escaped phased migration's Phase D smoke). **Lesson learned (filed for future Gate 11 candidacy, not formalized this sprint):** when migrating iframe → embedded, the Phase D smoke checklist must include a side-by-side visual diff with the standalone shell — same module, same backend, same theme — to catch resource-loading deltas. Gate 10 (Sprint 6.20) caught chrome position drift across pages; an analogous Gate 11 ("Embedded-host resource parity") would have caught this. Not formalized this sprint to keep hotfix surgical.

- Sprint 7.2 (PR #171) — **DEBT-2026-05-09-B architecture approval + Sprint 7.3 prompt creation**. Pure docs sprint: zero production code changed, zero tests changed. - Sprint 7.1 (PR #170) — **DEBT-2026-05-09-B discovery — vocabulary iframe → JS module architecture audit**. Pure discovery sprint: zero production code changed, zero tests changed. Phase A audit (Explore agent, 2h) mapped the current vocab cluster — parent `vocabulary.html` lazy-loads three child iframes (`my-vocabulary.html`, `flashcards.html`, `exercises.html`) with `?embedded=1`; embedded-mode IIFE on each child sets `html.embedded-mode` before CSS loads; `embedded-mode.css` (51 LOC) hides `.topnav-wrap` + banners via direct-child selectors (extended Sprint 6.17.1). The three children are **dual-use**: also linked standalone from `speaking.html` lines 937/954/978 + deep links from `d1-exercise.html`, `flashcard-study.js`, `my-vocabulary.js` — refactor must preserve standalone URLs as hard requirement. Backend API surface = 27 endpoints across `vocabulary_bank.py` (13) + `flashcards.py` (13) + `auth.py` (`/auth/me` for feature flags); **backend orthogonal to refactor, no changes needed**. State is per-page-isolated except `localStorage.av-theme` shared across all pages. Tests pinning iframe contract live in `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs:220-251` (embedded-mode IIFE byte-identical on children + `.topnav-wrap` selector in `embedded-mode.css`) and lines 264-306 (Gate 10 anchor sentinel). **4 architecture options analyzed** (Option A full-inline, Option B JS-module dynamic-import, Option C Web Components, Option D iframe-hybrid optimization). **Recommendation: Option B** — each child page module exports `mount(container, opts) → unmount()`; parent uses `await import()` to mount into tab containers; standalone HTML pages keep working as thin shells that mount the same module. Preserves dual usage cleanly, eliminates 3× chrome init overhead, retires `embedded-mode.css` at end of migration, compatible with Aver Design System light-DOM cascade. **Effort estimate: ~22h split across Sprint 7.3 (my-vocab module + parent API), 7.4 (flashcards module), 7.5 (exercises module + feature-flag IIFE migration), 7.6 (embedded-mode cleanup + final test pin updates)**. Phased over 4 PRs because each phase is independently shippable — parent keeps iframe path for unconverted tabs during migration. Sprint 7.2 = Andy approves architecture (30 min). **Frontend gate: 2752/2752 unchanged.** Audit hotfix count unchanged at 14 (Sprint 7.1 is discovery, not implementation). Phase A synthesis document committed at `docs/sprint-7-1-vocab-iframe-discovery.md`.
- Sprint 6.20 (PR #169) — **nav position drift surgical fix + Gate 10 formalization (cumulative 13 audit gates)**. Andy reported chrome shifts vertically by ~24px when navigating between pages — Codex visual consistency audit had reported Sprint 6.19 markup contract 9/9 GREEN, but the position-level drift slipped through because contract tests verify markup, not rendered pixel position. Phase A audit (Explore agent, 45 min) traced the root cause to a 2-of-18 page outlier: `home.html` and `vocabulary.html` nested `<nav class="topnav">` inside `<div class="shell">` (which has `padding-top: var(--av-space-6)` = 24px), while the other 16 canonical chrome pages use `<div class="topnav-wrap"><nav class="topnav">` as a direct body child (no top padding). Both wrappers declare identical `max-width: 1180px; margin: 0 auto`, so horizontal alignment was unaffected; only vertical drift manifested cross-page. Phase B Andy approved **Option A** (surgical HTML restructure of the 2 outlier pages — the canonical pattern is already proven on 16 pages, no CSS changes required, no per-page overrides needed). **Atomic fixes:** (1) **home.html** — `<nav class="topnav">` lifted out of `<div class="shell">` and wrapped in canonical `<div class="topnav-wrap">` as direct body child, before `.shell`; preserves Sprint 6.19 `.eyebrow` markup and Sprint 6.18 spacing tokens; (2) **vocabulary.html** — identical restructure pattern; (3) **DESIGN_SYSTEM.md § 17.14** — NEW Gate 10 (Visual position verification) formalized: origin Sprint 6.20 retrospection, applies to position-sensitive UI / sticky elements / cross-page consistent visual anchors / mixed canonical+bespoke layouts, verification protocol with per-page absolute position measurement at canonical viewport sizes (1440/768/375px), drift threshold >2px, manual smoke checklist template, anti-patterns documenting "markup-correct ≠ position-correct"; (4) **§ 17.12 evolution table** — extended from 5 → 6 blind-spot instances (Sprint 6.20 row added); intro updated "six sprints, six distinct mechanisms"; pattern principle list gained Gate 10 entry; (5) **§ 17.13 consolidation table** — cumulative gate count 12 → 13 with Gate 10 row formalized Sprint 6.20; methodology sections index gained § 17.14 entry. **Tests:** (1) NEW `gate-10-formalization.test.mjs` (12 pins) — § 17.14 section + origin + concept + viewport protocol + pages-list + § 17.12 (6 sprints + intro language + pattern principle) + § 17.13 (cumulative 13 gates + Gate 10 row + all 13 gates referenced) + methodology index; (2) extended `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` with Sprint 6.20 Gate 10 cross-page anchor sentinel (18 pins, one per canonical chrome page) verifying `.topnav-wrap` opens as a direct body child with no `.shell` / `<main>` / `<section>` / `<article>` ancestor open in `head` — HTML comments stripped before depth counting to neutralize Sprint 6.17.2 changelog snippets. **Frontend gate: 2752/2752 pins pass** (+30 net; 2722 → 2752). **Audit hotfix count 13 → 14** (Sprint 6.20 IS counted as audit hotfix because it formalized a new methodology gate, unlike fix sprints 6.17.x / 6.18 / 6.19 which preserved gate count). The chrome contract is now provably cross-page anchored — markup contract + Gate 10 sentinel + future visual smoke combine to prevent this drift class from recurring.
- Sprint 6.19 (PR #168) — **canonical subheading pattern + horizontal alignment + practice modes unification across the 18-page canonical chrome roster**. After Sprint 6.18 closed chrome vertical spacing, three remaining visual inconsistencies surfaced: (1) subheading drift — only 3/18 pages shipped a canonical eyebrow tier label (home, grammar landing, full-test-result, each with a different implementation); (2) horizontal alignment — needed to verify centered exceptions were intentional; (3) practice modes UI — Speaking's 4-tab sub-nav vs Grammar's 3 CTA hero buttons. Phase A audit (Explore agent, 45 min) classified 15/18 pages as MISSING eyebrow, confirmed 3 centered exceptions are intentional (grammar editorial, onboarding signup, full-test-result hero), and identified 4 distinct mode-switching patterns. Phase B Andy approved 4 decisions: (Q1) promote `.eyebrow` from home.css scoped rule to standalone canonical primitive in components.css; migrate `.ftr-eyebrow` page-hero to `.eyebrow` (section-level FTR eyebrows preserve `.ftr-eyebrow` for `--strength`/`--improve` modifier variants); (Q2) per-page eyebrow values (Speaking / Writing / Vocabulary / Grammar Wiki / Hồ sơ / Bắt đầu) + preserve "Overall Band Score" as page-specific domain context on FTR hero; (Q3) preserve grammar.html `.ds-badge.ds-badge-teal` editorial badge (§ 14.2 sub-system intentional — centered + editorial exception protected); (Q4) practice modes KEEP DIFFERENT (Speaking tabs = sub-nav semantic, Grammar buttons = hero CTA semantic — no unification). **Atomic fixes:** (1) **components.css** — canonical `.eyebrow` primitive added (font-size xs, semibold, tracking-widest, primary color, uppercase, margin-bottom space-3); (2) **15 pages gain `.eyebrow` markup:** speaking (×4 tab panels: Dashboard / Luyện tập / Luyện từng Part / Full Test), practice (in `.practice-context-bar`), result (in `.result-header`), full-test-result (in `.ftr-context-bar`), writing-dashboard, writing-result (in `.result-header`), vocabulary, my-vocabulary / flashcards / exercises (in their sticky context bars with `__sep` separator), profile, onboarding (step 1), grammar-roadmap, grammar-search, grammar-compare, grammar-article; (3) **full-test-result.html hero** — `.ftr-eyebrow` "Overall Band Score" class migrated to `.eyebrow`; section eyebrows (`.ftr-eyebrow--strength`, `.ftr-eyebrow--improve`, plain `.ftr-eyebrow`) preserved for distinct muted/success/warning styling; (4) **grammar.html** — NO CHANGES (Phase B Q3 editorial exception). **Tests:** NEW `subheading-pattern-canonical.test.mjs` (28 pins) — foundation `.eyebrow` primitive in components.css with canonical typography tokens, 17 per-page eyebrow text+class pins, FTR hero migration pin pair (canonical + no-regression), grammar.html editorial-badge preservation pin pair, practice modes distinct-pattern pin pair (speaking `.main-tab-nav` 4-tab + grammar `.btn-cta`), alignment exception triplet (grammar text-center + onboarding flex centering + FTR hero text-center). **Frontend gate: 2722/2722 pins pass** (+28 net; 2694 → 2722). Audit hotfix count unchanged at 13 (Sprint 6.19 is fix sprint, not audit hotfix). **Sprint 6.20+ deferred scope:** no follow-up sprint required from 6.19; the canonical chrome contract is now fully unified across the 18-page roster (chrome structure + spacing + subheading + alignment).
- Sprint 6.18 (PR #167) — **canonical chrome vertical spacing unification across the 18-page canonical chrome roster**. Andy reported visible vertical-rhythm drift across redesigned pages: chrome-to-content gaps ranged from 24px (writing-dashboard `py-6`) to 88px (canonical home `.shell` 24px + `.topnav` 64px margin-bottom). Phase A audit (30 min, Explore agent) classified 17/18 pages into 5 drift categories against home.html canonical reference. Phase B Andy approved 4 decisions: (Q1) add 4 new semantic spacing tokens to tokens.css; (Q2) normalize Cat E secondary nav stack to 64px; (Q3) fix Cat F flex-layout pages; (Q4) preserve grammar landing horizontal centering — Sprint 6.18 is vertical-only, Sprint 6.19 (deferred) owns horizontal alignment. **Atomic fixes:** (1) **tokens.css** — 4 canonical chrome spacing tokens declared (`--av-chrome-top-padding: var(--av-space-6)`, `--av-chrome-bottom-margin: var(--av-space-16)`, `--av-chrome-to-content-single: 88px`, `--av-secondary-nav-height: 48px`); (2) **Cat A** (5 pages: profile, writing-dashboard, my-vocabulary, flashcards, exercises) — Tailwind `py-N` wrapper symmetric shorthand replaced with explicit `pt-16/pt-20` + `pb-N` to compensate for absent `.shell` top padding; (3) **Cat B** (1 page: writing-result) — `main.result-content` top padding lifted from `--av-space-6` to `--av-space-20` (80px) to clear sticky `.result-tabs` band; (4) **Cat E** (8 pages: 5 grammar + practice + result + full-test-result) — secondary nav rules (`.gw-subnav`, `.practice-header`, `.result-header`, `.ftr-header`) ship `margin-bottom: var(--av-chrome-bottom-margin)` in their respective CSS files (grammar-wiki.css, practice.css, result.css, full-test-result.css); (5) **Cat F** (2 pages: speaking, onboarding) — speaking.css `.main-tab-nav` ships canonical margin-bottom; onboarding.html primary `<main>` gains `pt-20`. **Tests:** NEW `chrome-spacing-canonical.test.mjs` (42 pins) — foundation tokens declared, components.css `.shell`/`.topnav` unchanged, Cat A wrappers ship pt-N + pb-N (no symmetric py-N regression), Cat B writing-result CSS uses `--av-space-20`, Cat E secondary nav CSS rules use `var(--av-chrome-bottom-margin)`, Cat F speaking + onboarding canonical, 18-page roster coverage with canonical `.topnav` pre-req. **Frontend gate: 2694/2694 pins pass** (+42 net; 2652 → 2694). Audit hotfix count unchanged at 13 (Sprint 6.18 is fix sprint, not audit hotfix). **Sprint 6.19 deferred scope:** horizontal alignment + subheading patterns + grammar landing centered horizontal preservation — explicitly out-of-scope for Sprint 6.18.
- Sprint 6.17.2 (PR #166) — **post-merge visual regression fixes + Grammar cluster canonical migration (Cat 3 exclusion override)**. Three bugs surfaced after Sprint 6.17.1 merge: (Bug 1) `writing-dashboard.html` nav-links wrapped to 2 rows because the canonical `.topnav-wrap` was nested inside `<main class="max-w-3xl">` (768px constraint blocked the 1180px topnav max-width); (Bug 2) `speaking.html` SOON badges rendered with subtle visual drift from the home canonical due to Tailwind CDN preflight `*, ::before, ::after { border-color: currentColor }` reset overriding the `.locked::after` border shorthand; (Bug 3) Grammar Wiki cluster (5 pages) was Cat 3 excluded from Sprint 6.17 chrome unification per Phase A audit recommendation — Andy overrode the exclusion for IA consistency. **Atomic 3-item fix:** (1) `writing-dashboard.html` — lifted `.topnav-wrap` out of `<main class="max-w-3xl">` to be a direct body child (canonical max-width restored); (2) `components.css` `.nav-links .locked::after` — explicit `font-family: var(--av-font-sans)`, `font-weight: var(--av-fw-medium)`, `line-height: 1`, `border-width/style/color` (split from shorthand), and `box-sizing: border-box` to defensively neutralize Tailwind CDN preflight; (3) **5 grammar pages migrated to canonical full nav** (`grammar.html` + `grammar-roadmap.html` + `grammar-search.html` + `grammar-compare.html` + `grammar-article.html`; Grammar tab `.active`) with the editorial breadcrumb + stats badges preserved as a **secondary nav** (`<nav class="gw-subnav">`) directly below the canonical chrome — preserves Grammar Wiki's editorial-tier visual identity (DM Sans + Lora § 14.2 typography untouched, Sprint 6.15.7-hotfix layout-context replaced by canonical `.topnav-right` flex container which the structural sentinel already validates). **Tests:** `chrome-unification-canonical.test.mjs` `CANONICAL_CHROME_PAGES` extended from 13 → 18 (added 5 grammar pages); `cross-page-navigation-canonical.test.mjs` HREF_PINS updated to absolute `/pages/home.html` form on all 3 grammar entries; `theme-toggle-layout-context.test.mjs` Sprint 6.15.7-hotfix wrapper pin replaced by canonical `.topnav-right` flex-container pin (the structural sentinel above already covers all 29+ redesigned pages via `FLEX_HINTS`). **Frontend gate: 2652/2652 pins pass** (+40 net; 2612 → 2652). Audit hotfix count unchanged at 13 (Sprint 6.17.2 is fix sprint, not audit hotfix). **Cumulative chrome unification:** 5 Cat 1+2 reference pages (PR #164) + 10 Cat 2 student pages (PR #165) + 5 grammar pages (this PR) = **20 redesigned pages now on canonical full nav** with consistent skill discovery, user-pill dropdown, and logout flow.

## When to update this ledger

- After every per-page redesign sprint ship
- After every audit closure
- After every page deletion
- After every Phase closure milestone
- After Phase 5+ planning decisions
- Sprint hotfix prompts include a ledger-update step

This ledger is canonical for closure truth. Other docs (`DESIGN_SYSTEM.md` § 14, `UNIFIED_DESIGN_BRIEF.md` § 2, `CLAUDE.md` file-structure table) reference this file. If you find a closure claim somewhere else that contradicts this ledger, the ledger wins and the other doc should be corrected.
